In short, the government's position is now becoming more stable, and the Popular Action Party, which participated in the Lerroux cabinet, (that is, the Catholic Party led by Robles) will undoubtedly take the opportunity to develop. The current Spanish government and the majority party in parliament do not approve of the system of local autonomy. The political future will tend towards authoritarianism. Therefore, the failure of Catalonia this time has a great impact on the province's own position and the general politics of the country. This is what we can predict. (Havas Telegram dated the 7th)

Catalonia

Provincial Government Bombarded 27

Over Five Hundred Deaths

Central Government Appoints New Chairman

The situation in Madrid and Barcelona seems to have improved. The government has appointed Aleyna as the chairman of the Autonomous Government of Catalonia. The whole province is returning to normal, with only a few places experiencing shootings. (Havas News Agency, August 8th)

Government troops bombarded the Catalan government building, leaving bullet holes all over the walls, and the central balcony was also blown away, demonstrating the fierceness of the attack by the troops under General Batet. Catalan government Chairman Companys requested 3,000 soldiers stationed in Sabadell for assistance, but they were slow to arrive. Seeing that the situation was hopeless, he requested surrender. When Mr. Companys emerged from the devastated government building with his head held high, soldiers were lined up on both sides. Previous reports of his injury were inaccurate. It is now believed that Mr. Companys and other arrested leaders are being held in a ship in the port of Barcelona.

According to a Reuters report from Barcelona, it is now very dangerous to walk in the city because rebels are still hiding and engaging in sniping. Residents are lying on the ground floor all night to prevent stray bullets from hitting people from above. General Batet broadcast an order on the radio today, ordering residents to open all windows, otherwise they will be shot at. This is to prevent rebels from hiding by the windows and sniping. Rumors say that the government's bombing of the Catalan government building resulted in between five hundred and one thousand deaths, but the actual number of casualties cannot be determined at this time. (Reuters News Agency, August 7th)

Barcelona: After fierce fighting between the central government troops and the provincial troops, the provincial troops were defeated and have now surrendered. As of now, 34 people have died and many have been injured in the incident. 32 people are seriously injured. General Batet, the commander-in-chief of the central troops, has issued an order, ordering all workers and civil servants in the province to return to work tomorrow morning, and those who violate the order will be severely punished. Important officials of the autonomous province who have been arrested include Chairman Companys, Education Director Gasol, Finance Director Esteve, Provincial Assembly Speaker Mestre, and Guard Captain Farras. They are now all detained on the "Uruguay" ship. Gao Er, Director of the Public Security Bureau, and Lieutenant Colonel Ricardo, the police captain, are both missing. Former central government Prime Minister and left-wing leader Azaña is also missing. Mr. Azaña was not in the provincial government or the old governor's office last night. It is reported that before the central government announced martial law nationwide, Mr. Azaña had a long conversation with Chairman Companys of the autonomous government, expressed his disapproval of the incident, and predicted that the outcome would be a failure. Mr. Azaña then quietly withdrew because no one listened to him and sought a place to hide. The city has not yet returned to peace. A large store caught fire, and it is generally believed that anarchists took advantage of the chaos to commit arson and sabotage. Casualties in the turmoil:

Over Three Hundred Dead, Over One Thousand Injured 28

Madrid: Since the nationwide turmoil began last Thursday, a total of 350 people have died and 1,200 have been injured. The government has now been able to control the overall situation, but Asturias Province has not yet been pacified. (National News Agency, August 8th)

Regarding the failure in Catalonia, there is one small thing to record. Japanese Reform of Anti-Counterfeiting Agency Case

Sparking Secret Conflicts Between Military and Police 33

Police Oppose Commander of Military Police Governing Police Affairs

Settlers Petition Okada to Reconsider

Military Headquarter Is Hardline, Prime Minister Finds It Difficult To Please Both Sides

(Tokyo) The top leaders of the Colonial Affairs Ministry held a meeting at 6:00 PM yesterday. Mori Shige, the clerical official who returned to Tokyo on the 6th, and Hatta, the section chief who returned on the 7th, reported that local police officials were fiercely opposed to the commander of the Kwantung Army Military Police concurrently serving as the police chief of the Kwantung Government, and the situation was serious. The meeting did not end until 12:10 AM today. (Hualian News Agency, August 8th)

(Tokyo) Regarding the issue of reforming the agencies in Manchuria, the Ministry of Colonial Affairs listened to the results of the inspection of the actual situation in the Kwantung Government. As a result, the Vice Ministers Tsubouchi and Tanaka, along with section chiefs and lower officials of each bureau, discussed and decided to submit a written opinion to Okada, who concurrently serves as the Minister of Colonial Affairs. The local police officials' opinion on the reform issue is that they absolutely oppose the government's system of having the commander of the military police concurrently serve as the police chief, and the reform plan for the deployment. If the government forcibly implements it, it is unknown what will happen in the future, and even a bloody tragedy may occur. It is hoped that the government will take this into account, understand the actual situation on the ground, change its understanding, and reconsider the reform plan. (Dentsu News Agency, August 8th)

(Tokyo) The police officials of the Kwantung Government are vehemently opposed to the military police system. Although the attitude of the Ministry of the Army is also very tough, it is unwilling to show weakness in this regard and is still seeking to implement its claims. However, the reform plan for anti-counterfeiting is a decision of the Cabinet, and if it is modified, it will lead to political responsibility. Prime Minister Okada is in a difficult position to satisfy both sides, and it is attracting much attention from political parties as to how he will act. (Hualian News Agency, August 8th)

(Dalian) At the end of last week, Japanese police officers from 25 locations in Manchuria held a secret meeting in Lushun, deciding to form a united front to oppose Tokyo's plan to merge the police department into the Military Police Headquarters. A delegation of police officers went to Changchun this morning to meet with Hishikari, the Japanese ambassador to Manchuria and commander-in-chief of the Kwantung Army, to protest. The Japanese police in Manchuria are currently working as usual, but they are determined to implement their protest, at any cost. (Reuters News Agency, August 8th)

Japanese Ambassador to Germany

Explains Foreign Policy 34

Covering Up Aggression with Talk of Peace

(Berlin) The Japanese Ambassador to Germany, Nagai, recently gave a speech to representatives of the Berlin evening newspapers, explaining the situation in the Far East and the relationship between Japan and the League of Nations in Europe. He said, "Asia for Asians" is a slogan that is often misunderstood by the world. Asians do not want to completely break away from the "shackles" of Europe, but want to maintain and develop Asia's inherent culture so that all nations in the East and West can contribute greatly to world peace. Regarding the League of Nations, Japan has always been prepared to cooperate with Geneva in cultural undertakings, but in the political sphere, Japan refuses to cooperate with the League of Nations. Japan has nothing to do with the Gran Chaco incident, and whether it exports arms to Bolivia or Paraguay is irrelevant to Japan. This is why Japan ignores the League of Nations' resolution to ban the export of arms to Bolivia and Paraguay. When asked whether Japan supports using meetings or direct negotiations with foreign governments, he cannot generalize, but must consider the specific circumstances of each issue. In short, Japan is always prepared to cooperate in anything that is conducive to peace and culture, regardless of the means chosen. Finally, he said that the relationship between Japan and Germany is based on mutual respect. (Havas News Agency, August 8th)

(National News Agency, August 7th)

British Trial Planting of Soybeans

Manchurian Soybean Exports Will Be Affected 38

(London) Britain has never produced soybeans, and all domestic needs have been met by Manchuria. Now, soybeans are being planted on the farm of the American automobile tycoon Ford Company near Chelmsford, and there has been an excellent harvest. This is unprecedented in Britain. According to the Daily Express, the soybean harvest has already been completed on the farm's ten hectares. This experiment is very interesting and will be further developed in the future, and the scale will be expanded. The soil and climate of Britain are both suitable. The Ministry of Agriculture has received letters from the majority of farmers, believing that soybean imports amount to hundreds of thousands of tons each year. Now that they can be grown domestically, they should request the government to vigorously promote this crop. According to soybean experts, the beans planted by the Ford Company farm are of better quality than those produced in Manchuria. (Havas News Agency, August 8th)

Central Government/National Government

Two Memorial Week Reports 40

Ma Chaojun... Chinese Rural Economy

Sun Ke... Discussion of Draft Constitution

(Nanjing) At the 151st Memorial Week held by the Central Government at 9:00 AM on the 8th, Central Committee members Ye Chucang, Ma Chaojun, Li Ciwen, Chen Ce, and all staff members, totaling approximately 500 people, attended. Chairman Ye Chucang presided. Ma Chaojun reported on "The Reasons for the Collapse of the Chinese Rural Economy and the Principles of Relief," stating that the reason for the collapse of the Chinese rural economy is that the relationship between the supply and demand of agricultural labor in various provinces is not adapted. Many places lack agricultural labor, while many places have a surplus of agricultural labor. This type of maladaptation may be due to population, natural disasters, military service, low grain prices, or the loss of the Northeast on September 18th. However, the root cause of the rural collapse is not here, but because (1) there are too many farmers, (2) there is too little arable land, (3) the agricultural labor productivity is too small, (4) the productivity is too weak, and (5) the transportation costs are too expensive. The fundamental principle of relief is to develop agriculture and industries other than agriculture at the same time. The two must not be neglected in order to eliminate all the causes of the rural collapse. As for the capital for developing industries, the country must first be stabilized so that foreigners will be willing to invest, and then all industries can be built. The meeting adjourned after the speech. (Central News Agency, August 8th)

(Nanjing) The National Government held a Memorial Week at 8:00 AM on the 8th. Cao Haosen, Chen Qicai, Chen Xunyong, Lin Xiang, Lü Chao, Wei Huai and other staff members from various courts, ministries, and commissions, totaling more than 500 people, attended. After Chairman Lin led the ceremony, Sun Ke reported on the progress of the Legislative Yuan's discussion of the draft constitution, stating that since the opening of the meeting, the hospital has discussed the draft constitution, and has completed the discussion of Chapter 1 General Principles, Chapter 2 Rights and Obligations of the People, Chapter 3 National Congress, and Chapter 4 President, Executive Yuan, and Legislative Yuan, and passed the second reading. The remaining chapters will continue to be discussed, and the discussion will be completed in about a week. The most important parts of the draft constitution are (1) the abolition of the National Congress Committee, (2) the President's powers, in addition to being the head of state, also serve as the head of the Executive Yuan, with overall executive power, (3) the central government of the Five-Power Constitution is formed by the President and the presidents of the five houses, and not a single unit is the central government, and (4) the powers of the central and local governments are based on the Three People's Principles and adopt a balanced power system. (Central News Agency, August 8th)

Shicheng Public

Warmly Welcome the National Army 41

The Eastern Route Army Advances to Hetian; Recovering Key Points in Eastern Tingzhou

(Nanchang) Since the capture of Shicheng on the morning of the 6th, the local people have warmly welcomed the National Army, with a continuous stream of people offering condolences and support. They also earnestly requested the dispatch of troops to quickly suppress the remaining bandit areas that have not yet been recovered. Division Commander Sun Yuanliang, in addition to providing proper reassurance, also instructed nearby troops to assist the people with the autumn harvest. (Central News Agency, 8th)

(Nanchang) Liao Shiqiao telegraphed from the east (1st) stating that approximately one thousand bandits of the pseudo-Expeditionary Army, with about four hundred rifles, had fled from Guichi to Zhide on the (25th). They were then pursued southward via Shatan by two battalions of troops. On the 27th, they were engaged near Taoshu Shop, resulting in four hours of intense fighting, after which they were routed and fled. The pursuing battalions continued their pursuit along different routes, causing the bandits to become even more disorganized, fleeing into the deep mountains and forests. The search and suppression are still underway. It is estimated that over a hundred bandits were killed on the spot and along the route. That evening, another two hours of intense fighting took place at Sucun Slope, resulting in the death of over thirty bandits, the seizure of eleven rifles, several mules and horses, and the capture of six male and female bandits, etc. (Central News Agency, 8th)

(Nanchang) According to a telegram report from the Eastern Route Army Headquarters (1st), the pseudo-supervisor Chen Chengen confessed as follows: (1) The pseudo-9th Army Corps only commands the 3rd Division, which has no division commander and is directly commanded by Luo Binghui. The pseudo-3rd Division has three infantry regiments, one special service, one guard, one communications, and one engineering company each. Each company has approximately fifty rifles, with each rifle carrying ten rows of ammunition. (2) Soldiers are given a daily allowance of 14 cents. Rice is forcibly requisitioned from residents, and salt is looted from Zhanghuban. They are only barely fed three meals a day, causing great suffering. They are only held in check by heavy constraints, making it impossible to escape. (3) In the Battle of Kuzhu, the 3rd Battalion of the pseudo-7th Army Corps suffered heavy casualties, with only one company remaining. The pseudo-Military Commission strictly ordered them to defend the fortifications west of Wenfang to the death, with Luo Binghui personally supervising the battle. (4) In the Battle of Zhongwu Village on the (30th), the pseudo-9th Army Corps and the pseudo-24th Division suffered consecutive defeats over several days, with more than half of their troops killed or wounded, etc. (Central News Agency, 8th)

(Nanchang) When our army killed Zhang Sheng, the battalion commander of the pseudo-3rd Division, they found a pseudo-instruction from bandit leader Peng Dehuai. It described the impact of pseudo-officers and soldiers surrendering and providing information, and the lack of fighting spirit due to the disintegration of the bandit army. This proves that their total collapse is not far off. Furthermore, according to a telegram from Zhou Hunyuan to the Executive Headquarters, many bandit soldiers are currently unwilling to fight, but they are being monitored by ten-man squads everywhere, making it impossible to surrender. (Central News Agency, 8th)

(Wuhu)徽 Bandit Luo Binghui was severely attacked by the 7th Army, with two pseudo-division commanders killed and even more captured. He has fled into the mountains on the border of Fujian and Jiangxi. (Special Dispatch, 8th)

(Fuzhou) Key points such as Hetian Guanqian Nanshan Ba have been recovered. The pseudo-9th Army Corps and 24th Division initially resisted stubbornly based on the terrain, but were ultimately defeated. The National Army is now advancing towards Tingzhou to attack. As the various bandit areas are being successively recovered, the Provincial Government has specifically formulated ten measures to urge wealthy people to return to their hometowns, requiring wealthy people who have left their hometowns to move back within three months. If they are unable to move back due to circumstances, they must appoint a representative to manage their property and business, and report to the district public office, which will then forward the information to the county for record-keeping. Otherwise, the county government may, at the request of the district chief, seal and manage their property or business. (Special Dispatch, 8th)

(Nanjing) Zhou Hunyuan telegraphed on the 30th, stating that his troops attacked the bandit's strong fortifications on the high ground around Gaoxingxu Shixingshan and its vicinity on the morning of the 30th. The bandits stubbornly resisted from the fortifications. After our officers and soldiers bravely and fiercely attacked, a fierce battle ensued, and the bandits were finally defeated. More than 30 bandit fortifications were occupied one after another. The bandits could not withstand the attack and fled to the area south of Gaoxingxu. After our troops fiercely pursued, they were in a miserable state, suffering extremely heavy casualties. By noon, all the attacked areas were completely occupied. In this battle, a total of over 1,000 bandits were killed, and over 400 people, including the regimental political commissar, were captured, along with four light and heavy machine guns and over 400 rifles. The bandits engaged in this battle were identified as the 12th and 2nd divisions, the strongest combat forces of the bandits, and they were not even worth a single blow. This shows that the bandit army is in disarray and its total collapse is not far off. (Special Dispatch, 7th)

(Fuzhou) The military operations to suppress bandits in Fujian are progressing smoothly. According to combined military intelligence, the bandits have built several lines of defense in Pengkou Liancheng Xidi. The first line, along Chengxi Datoukeng Jingbaishi Naolong Naoling, serves as their forward defense line. The second line, along Taipingling Zhishuling Qiaoxia Dong Jinhuashan Zhu Zailing Baiyi Yangling Baxian , stretches for fifty miles and is their main fortified defense line. Furthermore, west of Zhongwu Village, across the north and south high mountains of Hengyi , stretches dozens of miles, forming their third line of defense. Nanshan Ba Daluowu's north and south high grounds form their fourth line of defense. Our Second Route Army began its attack on the 26th of last month, occupying the bandit's forward defense line on the same day. On the 27th, they continued to attack the bandit's main defense line, first capturing Baiyi Yangling, then capturing Qili Hengpai Shanggulouling, attacking the left flank of the bandits. More than 700 bandit corpses were found in their trenches. On the 28th, they continued to attack Songmaoling, Zhu Zailing, Jinlongshan Qiaoxia and other places, all of which were successively recovered. On the 29th, the battlefields were cleared, and fortifications and pillboxes were constructed at the same time. On the 30th, the bandits in the Huangyi Nan area were attacked, and the newly recovered areas were occupied on the 1st and 2nd to construct fortifications. On the 3rd, a fierce attack was launched on the bandit's fourth line of defense at Nanshan Ba, which was finally recovered by noon on the 4th. The remaining bandits fled backwards, and our army has occupied the key points of various villages east of Changting. They are now advancing to Hetian, and the recovery of Changting is no longer a problem. (Central News Agency, 8th)

Luo's bandits, holed up in Changting, have four lines of defense, with Zhongxing Village as the first line, Nanshan Ba as the second line, Hetian as the third line, and the Widow's Bridge area outside Changting City as the fourth line. The Eastern Route Army occupied Zhongwu Village on the 29th and attacked Nanshan Ba on the 4th, which can be captured soon. Although the third line of Shatian has no high mountains, and there is the danger of the Tingjiang River, it is not difficult to attack and directly strike Changting. It is only a matter of time. In Principle, There Should Be No Major Modifications to the

Savings Bank Law 48

Ma Yinchu's Remarks

Responsible Official of the Ministry of Finance Discusses

Disaster Relief Measures for Various Provinces 49

(Nanjing) The water and drought disasters in various provinces in the north and south this year are severe. The government has ordered them to report separately so that land taxes can be reduced or exempted. The Relief Commission, together with the Ministries of Interior and Finance, has discussed and drafted measures. According to a responsible official of the Ministry of Finance, the Relief Commission of the Ministry of Interior has investigated and found that the drought damage in provinces such as Jiangsu, Zhejiang, and Anhui is over 50%. The flood damage in provinces such as Hebei, Chahar, and Shandong is less than 50%. Because the Relief Commission has received many requests for relief from various parties, it has consulted with the Ministry several times. However, the disaster situation is too severe, and relief measures have not yet been agreed upon. As for disaster relief measures, in 1930, the National Government ordered the central government to allocate 1% of its annual income and the provincial and county governments to allocate 2% annually as disaster relief funds. It was also stipulated that disasters with damage below 50% would be relieved with local funds, and disasters with damage above 50% would be relieved with funds allocated by the central government if local funds were insufficient. The Ministry, based on these regulations, has ordered the affected provinces to first raise funds locally for relief. If that is insufficient, the central government will raise funds or purchase seeds. As for the reduction or exemption of land taxes, the reports from various provinces are complete, and orders for implementation will be issued separately after review. (Special Dispatch, 8th)

Unease on the Border of the Puppet State (Harbin Correspondence) 92

Manzhouli is Calm on the Surface

Dakerh is Heavily Fortified

The news heard in Harbin is inevitably one-sided, but the tension of the Japanese army can be seen from their actions. There is no doubt that they are preparing to deal with any unexpected events at any time. However, there is a strange thing here, that is, Manzhouli, the northwest border pass of the three eastern provinces, is very calm on the Japanese side. There are very few troops stationed there, as if they have not actively set up defenses. Judging from this point, there is no intention of war on the surface, and the Japanese there have expressed their safety, engaging in the development of the forests and minerals buried in the nearby mountains and rivers, as well as aquatic resources, implicitly showing that they want to

compete with the Soviet Union in developing Siberia.

At first, we felt this was very strange. Why did the Soviet Union gather the Transbaikal Military District, stationing more than nine infantry regiments, seven cavalry regiments, distributing 120 artillery pieces, more than 60 aircraft, three tank squadrons, three armored trains, fifteen armored vehicles, and one chemical warfare battalion, as well as several G.P.U. (Political Security Team) units in areas such as Da Uli and Aba Heights? Behind these troops are two major air force bases, Irkutsk and Nizhneudinsk. Tomsk, Omsk, Novosibirsk, and other places are all heavily garrisoned, serving as a reserve team for the Far East. If something happens, they can be concentrated in Chita in an instant. We tried to climb the small mountains near Manzhouli to see, and we could see neatly arranged barracks on the opposite Russian territory, with steel-reinforced concrete fortresses everywhere.

The impetuous and war-loving Japanese, witnessing this situation and hearing that the Siberian Railway is laying double tracks and working day and night, how can they be so calm to deal with it, or be dedicated to the basic work of the economy? After repeated investigations by reporters, they learned that the Japanese army believes that Manzhouli is backed by Hulun Lake, and the Ergun River is a position with its back to the water. If they want to defend this place or use it as a base for attack, it is strategically disadvantageous. Therefore, they do not set up defenses in Manzhouli or Hailar, acting out a peaceful appearance and creating a military intention. They have built all the military fortresses in the Greater Khingan Mountains. These mountain borders and forest edges not only have solid fortresses and hidden trenches, but also have anti-aircraft gun positions.

The most important work is that the Hailar River, Gen River, and Derbul River all widely cultivate White Russian people. They have a deep hatred for the Soviet Union and almost cannot coexist with the Red Party.

The Japanese comforted them in every way, wanting them to be used by Japan in the future. Now they are being driven by the Japanese side. These people who have fled to foreign countries also want to turn over, so they are willing to listen.

In fact, the military focus, whether on the Soviet or Japanese side, once war is used, the center of the war, land battle, is not in Manzhouli in the west, nor in Suifenhe in the east, but in Daheihe on the Heilongjiang bank near Heilongjiang Province. About eighty miles downstream of Heihe is the famous Aihui City. Across a river about one mile wide is the Soviet territory of Hailanpao. If Japan adopts an offensive, it will inevitably use the Tao'ang Road, Huhai Road, and the under-construction Erzhan-Heihe Railway, cross the river to the east, break through the Hailanpao defense line, and cut off the connection between the Ussuri Railway and the Siberian Railway, so that the coastal province and the Transbaikal region cannot echo each other. The commander of the Far East Army in Boli cannot command the entire army, and the Japanese army can attack Vladivostok by sea and land, seizing the East and West Siberian regions as appropriate. The Soviet Union is probably also focusing on Hailanpao, quickly crossing the Heilongjiang River, breaking through Heihe, crossing the Lesser Khingan Mountains, and going south to Keshan to spy on Harbin, and attacking Longjiang to the west to attack Taonan. This is a place they must fight for. Therefore, Japan is heavily garrisoned in Heihe and Aihui, and builds a transportation network. The defenses of the Lesser Khingan Mountains

Although not very thorough, it is also paying attention to planning strict precautions, fearing that Heihe will be lost and the entire line of the three eastern provinces will be shaken.

The triangular area where the Songhua River and Heilongjiang River meet has many disputes and is more likely to cause problems. At the Sanhekou, both sides have wire fences, and there is also police on land. The Japanese also use the name of the puppet on the water, equipped with two large 900-ton gunboats, four gunboats carrying eight guns, eight small 100-ton gunboats, and two small aircraft carriers carrying aircraft, carrying 80 seaplanes, specializing in monitoring Soviet smuggling and striving for military advantages. However, the Soviet side is also heavily guarded and will not easily let the Japanese army fly over. The two sides confront each other, and everyone wants to grasp the military advantage and establish a solid military base is obvious. (October 1)

Three Route Army Recaptures Shicheng 93

丨Changting and Xingguo Will Also Be Taken Soon丨

Nanchang Correspondence: The headquarters has just received a phone call from the Three Route Army from the front line stating that Shicheng County was completely recaptured at approximately 5:00 AM on the 6th.

The details are as follows:

Previously, the Red Bandits used Shicheng to connect Jiangxi and Fujian, with Guangchang to the north, Ruijin to the south, Changting and Ninghua to the east,

and Ningdu to the west, serving as a connected area for the bandit areas in eastern Jiangxi, southern Jiangxi, western Fujian, and northern Jiangxi after the loss of Guangchang. Zhu De and Mao Zedong specially deployed the pseudo-Third Army Corps as the main force in the mountainous area along the border between Guangchang and Shicheng, Zhihua front, building a network of fortifications extending twenty miles in length and width.

Blockhouses and trenches were intertwined, and the defense was extremely tight. The Three Route Army successively fought multiple bloody battles with the pseudo-4th, 5th, 15th, and other divisions. The fortifications near Zhihua front were violently bombed by the Nationalist army's artillery and aircraft, and were completely destroyed. Starting on the 26th of last month, our various divisions launched an attack on the bandit positions in Zhonghua Mountain, Zhongzi Village, and other areas north of Shicheng, capturing two or thirty bandit blockhouses in succession. On the 30th, they arrived at Xiaosongshi. Peng Dehuai's forces were repeatedly defeated under the control of the Nationalist army's infantry, artillery, and air force, and their spirit was completely lost. The Nationalist army took advantage of the victory to advance and directly attacked Shicheng County. At that time, the pseudo-13th Army Corps and the pseudo-25th Division, which were defending the city, still attempted to fight with their backs to the city. On the 5th of this month, the Nationalist army launched an attack on the city, and completely occupied the county seat at dawn on the 6th. The remnants of the bandits retreated from the Xincun area west of Shicheng to the border of Ningdu. It has been seven years since Shicheng fell into the hands of bandits in 1928, and it has finally seen the light of day. The newly appointed Shicheng County magistrate, someone, had previously been stationed in Yiqian to work, and has now entered the city with the army to handle the aftermath.

Xingguo, Changting, and Gulonggang in Xingguo were recaptured in the same period as Shicheng. The East Route Army has advanced to a certain place west of Hetian, and Tingcheng is in sight. Recapturing should occur within a few days.

The main force of the pseudo-22nd, 3rd, and other divisions of Xingguo has long been defeated by the Nationalist army. Approaching the county seat, capturing it is only a matter of time. Gulonggang is a key area for entering Ningdu City. The Nationalist army has completely conquered the bandit positions and fortifications west of Gulonggang, and the Yonglong Road is also largely completed. (October 6)

Chiang Kai-shek Summoned Zhang Xueliang and He Chengjun

To Discuss the Aftermath of the Bandit Areas in Detail 94

The generals were given strategies and returned to their defenses immediately.

It is expected that the remnants of the bandits in the border areas will be completely eliminated within three months.

The General Headquarters decided to attend and instruct the expanded memorial week.

Hankou Correspondence: After Chairman Chiang arrived in Hankou from Xunyang a few days ago, he immediately convened a meeting of generals in Hankou to instruct on the details of clearing the remnant bandits in the border areas, and the general arrangements have been made. On the morning of the 7th, Chiang Kai-shek read important documents at the headquarters and individually summoned the generals of the various armies, Xu Yuanquan, Shangguan Yunxiang, Liu Maoen, Hao Mengling, Wang Yizhe, He Zhuguo, Liang Guanying, etc., and once again gave them strategies, ordering them to eliminate the remnant bandits in the shortest possible time. He also ordered that the construction of highways and blockhouses in the defense areas of the various armies should be completed quickly in accordance with the prescribed period, so that local security could be permanently consolidated. That noon,

He also summoned Zhang Xueliang and He Chengjun to discuss the implementation steps of the aftermath in detail, which lasted a long time. At 1:00 PM, Chiang Kai-shek and his wife, Ms. Soong Mei-ling, departed from the headquarters, went to the Jianghan Customs, patrolled the Jianghan Road, crossed the Xunlimen Railway to the Zhongzheng Road area, and then turned to Zhongshan Road through Qiaokou, passed the French Concession, and returned to the headquarters. At that time, the British Consul General in Hankou, Hilder, and the German Consul General, Timm, had a long friendship with Chairman Chiang Kai-shek, and were going to the headquarters to pay their respects. Chiang Kai-shek immediately prepared dishes and refreshments to entertain them, and summoned the mayor of Hankou, Wu Guozhen, to host them.

At 6:00 PM, Hilder and Timm departed. Chiang Kai-shek and his wife, Ms. Soong Mei-ling, went to Zhongshan Park for sightseeing, lingering among the forests, springs, pavilions, and terraces. When they had had their fill of pleasure, they returned to the headquarters, which was already illuminated by thousands of lights. The Wuhan General Headquarters decided to hold an expanded memorial week for Dr. Sun Yat-sen on the 8th, and earnestly requested Chairman Chiang Kai-shek to attend and instruct. It has been approved. The General Affairs Department of the General Headquarters specially notified the party, government, military, and academic institutions in Wuchang, Hanyang, and Hankou on the 7th, saying, "It has been found that next Monday, that is, at 9:00 AM on the 8th, this headquarters will hold an expanded memorial week. It has been ordered that all party, government, military, police, and academic institutions in Wuchang, Hanyang, and Hankou should come to participate, and so on. In addition to sending separate letters, this letter is hereby sent for reference. Please check the separately opened regulations for each level and arrive at the headquarters auditorium on time to participate. The participating institutions are as follows: members of the provincial party headquarters and above, members of the municipal party headquarters and above, officials with senior appointments and above in the Hubei Provincial Government, branch chiefs of the Hubei Provincial Public Security Bureau and above, branch chiefs of the Hankou Municipal Public Security Bureau and above, directors of all public security bureaus in Hubei Province, director of the Xiang'e-Ping-Han Railway Bureau, and members of the special party headquarters of the two railway bureaus, directors and deputy directors of the Anti-Smoking Supervisory Office, and head of the patrol regiment, colonels and above in the Pacification Headquarters, colonels and above in the Wuhan Garrison Command, principals of middle schools and above in Wuyang and Xia, please have the Hubei Provincial Government notify the captain and deputy captain of the Fourth Air Force Team, the stationmaster of the Hankou Air Station, captains and above of the naval fleet office, and directors of the offices of the military division stationed in Hankou and above, please have the Pacification Headquarters notify the director of the Third Recruitment Office, the director of the Hanyang Arsenal, and officers of this headquarters with the rank of major and above." The senior generals will also return to their defenses separately after participating in the memorial week. Because Chairman Chiang Kai-shek has to rush to Luoyang before the Double Ten Festival to attend the opening ceremony of the Central Military Academy branch school, he cannot stay in Hankou for long. He has decided to take a special train on the Pinghan Railway to Zhengzhou and transfer to Luoyang on the evening of the 8th. Zhang Xueliang will accompany him. He will still return to Hankou in about a few days. The plan for clearing the remnant bandits in the border areas of Henan, Hubei, and Anhui that Chairman Chiang Kai-shek and Zhang Xueliang have agreed upon this time is extremely detailed. If it is earnestly implemented, it is expected that the effect of clearing the area can be achieved within three months. (7th)

Yinjiang

Zhang Danhua Did Indeed Commit Suicide Due to Illness

Zhang Danhua, a resident of West Street, died from a gunshot wound due to illness. Various newspapers have reported this. At the time, the local news spread that Zhang had committed suicide. Relatives and friends in the city believed that Zhang was usually open-minded and would never commit suicide, and they did not believe it. Yesterday (the 6th), his sister went to the countryside and obtained two suicide notes, both addressed to his sister, instructing her to handle the funeral arrangements.

The reason for the suicide was that the long-term illness was difficult to cure and unbearable pain. He also asked the Jingshen Society Daoyuan to conduct a requiem for the deceased and not report it to the authorities for an autopsy. Both were addressed to his relative Xue Qiao, entrusting him to manage all rent matters and requesting him to continue to collect them on his behalf. Moreover, the state of death was extremely tragic. He used a self-defense pistol to hold the gun with his right hand and aimed it at his temple. The bullet entered from the right temple and exited from behind his left ear. The entrance wound was very small, and the exit wound was about half an inch. His hands were crossed, the pistol fell on his right arm, and the pillow and bedding were stained with blood. He was coffined by his sister and transported out on the 7th,

And placed in the funeral home outside the south gate. Those who knew Zhang in the past all sighed that Zhang's ending was so unexpected.

Wuxi

Robberies by Land and Water Occur Continuously 95

Recently, bandits have been uneasy and rampant. Four cases have occurred in just two days. (1) There were two sailing boats each between Wuxi and Panjiaqiao and Zhouqiao, which belong to Wujin County.

On the afternoon of the 5th of this month, the two sailing boats simultaneously departed from Wu and headed to Wuxi. At about 2:00 AM that night, when they sailed to the Maopeng Lane area near Zhangshe in Wuxi, they suddenly encountered a bandit boat, and more than a dozen bandits rushed out, holding two pistols.

They robbed the boats, losing seven or eighty yuan. (2) The sailing boats in Dangkou Town, District 8, travel between Suzhou and Dangkou without interruption. The night before last, they opened to Suzhou as usual. When they traveled to Feijiawei, they also encountered two bandit boats, and more than a dozen bandits robbed the native boats, losing more than one hundred yuan. (3) At 12:00 AM on the 6th, eight or nine bandits suddenly came to the house of the late resident Xia Jinwan in Laoxizhuang, North Extension City, District 8. They wrapped their heads in blue cloth, spoke in a strong northern accent, and broke open the gate to enter, rummaging through boxes and cabinets, and arbitrarily searching. They robbed about seven or eight hundred yuan in cash, foreign currency, and jewelry. (4) About three miles away from Laoxizhuang, the Yuantong Nunnery was also robbed by five or six bandits, losing seventy or eighty yuan.

Disputes Arise Again in the Automobile Industry 96

The local business automobiles had previously had disputes with the Xicheng Long-Distance Automobile Company's illegal collection of tolls, resulting in repeated disputes, unanimous strikes, and filing petitions with the provincial and county authorities. Later, Shen Qi, the director of the Provincial Highway Administration, personally came to Wuxi to handle the matter, and an compromise solution was agreed upon, and the disputes were resolved. However, since the resumption of business automobiles, the long-distance company still does not calculate the collection of tolls according to kilometers, but according to station names. For example, five jiao is charged to Tangtou Station, and five jiao is also charged to stations such as Xizhang Wangzhuang and Hujia Ferry, which has once again aroused the opposition of the automobiles. They convened an emergency meeting yesterday to discuss countermeasures, advocating that the toll be calculated at 1.5 fen per kilometer, and decided to appeal to the authorities for relief again, and vowed not to stop until the goal is achieved.

Danyang

Former Agricultural Bank President Arrested for Malpractice 97

Zhang Hanlin, the former president of the local Farmers Bank, was thoroughly investigated by Luo Meizhong and others who were sent by the provincial government and the Agricultural Bank headquarters to Danyang, and it was learned that Zhang had committed private malpractice before taking office. Chairman Chen of the provincial government telegraphed Chairman Liu of Anhui Province to detain him, welcome him to the province, and bring him back to the county for investigation in accordance with the law. Now, County Magistrate Bi has notified the local cooperative societies to report whether there are any funds involved and corruption. There are several companies such as Miaoduan Credit Cooperative that have submitted reports to the authorities. At 3:00 PM yesterday, Xu Cheng, the trial judge, held a hearing and questioned them. As a result, he instructed each to provide witnesses and to bring the accounts to the court for review. Zhang Hanlin was sent into custody, and another hearing was scheduled.

Joint Suppression of Sea Bandits by Water and Land Police Corps 98

Large groups of sea bandits have invaded the coastal areas of Tong, and used local cannons to bombard the shore. The Nantong District Security Command immediately mobilized the provincial and county water and land police corps to jointly suppress them. The bandit forces were unable to resist and retreated to the north. The martial law has not yet been lifted in each area.

Qingjiang

Resolution to Dredge Seven Major River Ports 99

The county government held the 49th district chief meeting yesterday afternoon at 2:00 PM to discuss the issue of dredging the major river ports in the county. It was resolved that the seven major river ports such as Jingjie River, Yubu Port, Miaoshu Port, Zhongtiansheng Port, Bawu Port, Yudai River, and Lingjing Port (southern section) should be dredged first. The district offices should expedite the submission of the registers for requisitioning labor and substitute money in accordance with the dredging regulations, taking into account past practices, so as to take advantage of this slack season to engage in dredging.

Jiashan

Robbery Case Near Tianning Town 100

Xu Changfa, a Shaoxing native who is a small business owner in the Lujiagang area, about three miles away from Tianning Town,

Had sold twenty-three piculs of white rice the day before, receiving 140 yuan, which was seen by bandits. The next night, when the fish jumped three times, more than a dozen bandits, with black cloths wrapped around their heads and carrying sharp weapons, swarmed to Xu's house, opened the gate, and ransacked the boxes and cabinets at will. They robbed more than 300 silver yuan. The local water police learned of this and went to arrest them, but the bandits had already fled without a trace.

Jiaxing

Verdict on Embezzlement Case at the Agricultural Bank 101

Following the major robbery that occurred at the Jiaxing Farmers Bank on August 15th, the Provincial Committee investigated and discovered embezzlement. Bank employees Xu Shuxiang and Ceng Yishan, along with laborers Tu Haihai and Jiang Shiyuan, were handed over to the court for investigation. The investigative authorities also apprehended suspects Feng Xingsun, Chen Afa, Zhi Asi, Tu Amao, and Jin Shi, who were also handed over to the court for interrogation and subsequently prosecuted according to the law. After repeated trials by Judge Zhou Wending of the Criminal Division, and after lawyers for each side presented their arguments, the court delivered its verdict on the morning of the 8th. Xu Shuxiang and Ceng Yiran were each sentenced to six months of imprisonment for the crime of embezzlement. Feng Xingsun and Chen Afa were each sentenced to two months of imprisonment for assisting in theft. Jin Shi, Tu Haigen, Song Shiyuan, Zhi Asi, and Shu Amao were acquitted. The related civil lawsuit portion was secretly transferred to the Civil Division for handling. Xu and Ceng both declared their dissatisfaction with the verdict in court.

They will appeal.

Premier Sun Yat-sen's London Peril 108

Meeting to be held at 11:00 AM

The whole city to fly flags at half-mast with heightened vigilance

The Guomin News Agency reports that the 11th is the anniversary of Sun Yat-sen's peril in London, when Mr. Sun Zhongshan was targeted by the Qing government for his revolutionary activities. The City Party Headquarters, to commemorate the great fearless spirit of Sun's late years, and per the methods set forth by the central government, will convene representatives from all sectors of the city to hold a commemorative meeting in the auditorium. All agencies, groups, schools, and party headquarters at all levels throughout the city will fly flags at half-mast in remembrance. Because this day is a revolutionary memorial day, the Shanghai-Songhu Garrison Headquarters and the Municipal Public Security Bureau are deeply concerned that reactionary elements may take the opportunity to cause trouble and have ordered their affiliated gendarmerie and district detachments to maintain strict vigilance. All inspectors, detectives, and male and female inspectors are being dispatched separately.

Together with the long-term police dispatched by each district office, sentries and posts will be added at the borders between the Chinese and foreign concessions and at all major roads, and pedestrians will be inspected. The police authorities in the two concessions, in order to prevent problems before they occur, have also increased the number of detectives patrolling the streets, paying particular attention to the areas near factories and schools, in order to curb the seeds of disorder.

Anqin Leaves Shanghai Today 111

Traveling to Hong Kong and Then to Tibet on Italian Ship

The Living Buddha Anqin Hutuktu, after arriving in Shanghai on the 3rd with more than 30 followers, responded to the invitation of the Buddhist community in Shanghai and gave a four-day Dharma teaching at the Buddhist Jingye Society on Hed Road, starting on the 5th. Many people went to receive the Dharma every day. The Dharma teaching ceremony was completed yesterday, so the Anqin Lama is scheduled to leave Shanghai today with Secretary-General Wang Luojie and more than 30 chanting Khenpos on the Italian Postal Ship Company's Conte Verde, traveling to Hong Kong. All luggage and tickets were entrusted to China Travel Service yesterday for processing. It is understood that after arriving in Hong Kong, the Anqin Lama will transfer to a ship to Kolkata, then travel to Tibet via India to arrange for the Panchen Lama to enter Tibet. He is scheduled to return to Beijing for reporting in February next spring. The city's party and government agencies and Buddhist groups will send personnel to greet him at that time.

Another Group Arrived Yesterday

Difficult Overseas Chinese in Japan Arrive in Shanghai 114

Appealed to the City Party Headquarters Yesterday

According to Shen Shi News Agency, another group of overseas Chinese expelled from Japan arrived in Shanghai on the Japanese ship Asama Maru on the 3rd of this month. The total is Wu Wentian, Xu Baonian, Xu Zijin, Sun Dianzhong, Ma Zuofa, Ji Yulai, Xia Zhongxing, Chen Anhai, Zhou Chengzhai, etc. Three people from Taizhou have already returned to their hometown. Among the above-mentioned people, there are five from Huzhou and four from Qingtian. They are now staying at the Daxin Inn in this city. A reporter from Shen Shi News Agency went to inquire about the situation.

Expelled from Japan and Returned to China 115

Those who were forced to return to China after being expelled from Japan this time

are mostly workers, with sugar and coal workers being the majority. Most of them were engaged in small businesses in Tokyo, Nagoya, and other places, with a population of over a thousand households. They were usually envied by the Japanese, who often extorted money from them or searched their homes in the middle of the night. If they found silver dollars, they would take them away. If there were none, they would whip and scold them. This time, after being driven back to China, they were beaten and imprisoned in a dark room. Two days later, Japanese police were sent to escort them onto the ship. Their clothes, if of some value, were stripped off. Food and accommodation on the ship were mostly provided by Chinese sailors. The overseas Chinese had no freedom to organize or assemble in Japan, so the embassy had no knowledge of the expulsion of the overseas Chinese.

Petitioned the City Party Headquarters 116

At 8:00 AM yesterday morning, Wu Wentian, Xu Baonian, Xu Zijin, and others led all the overseas Chinese to petition the City Party Headquarters. Yu Yaoqiu of the Party Headquarters received them and promised to introduce them to the Overseas Chinese Affairs Commission for reception. The text of their petition is recorded as follows: "Submitting this petition because of bankruptcy and destitution, we humbly request that you grant us relief to save our lives. We, Wentian, etc., have been running stores and working as sugar and coal workers in Tokyo City, Minami-Senju Town, Nagoya, and other places in Japan for more than ten years. We have followed the rules and regulations and have not committed any illegal acts. Unexpectedly, the Japanese coveted our rights and interests and suddenly, in September, many police officers came and forced us to return to China. We repeatedly requested that they return our accounts and sell our equipment,

so that we could use it as travel expenses. The police turned a deaf ear. If we delayed for a moment,

they would use their fists and feet, or even wooden sticks and gun handles, to beat us arbitrarily. Such rampant and unreasonable behavior is beyond description. We had no choice but to follow them to the police station for more than ten days, where we were not treated as human beings. All the silver dollars in our pockets were confiscated. Those who had married Japanese women were not allowed to bring them back to China. As a result, our clothes were taken off and sold to buy boat tickets. Although we have now arrived in Shanghai, we are unfamiliar with the place, have no clothes to keep us warm, no food to eat, and no place to live. We are wandering on the streets, and our lives are in danger. Fortunately, the owner of an old public inn,

out of sympathy for his fellow countrymen, has temporarily taken us in. Therefore, we are forced to request your assistance, to issue us travel expenses and boat tickets,

so that we, difficult overseas Chinese drifting overseas, can return to our homeland and save our lives. This would be truly virtuous."

Juxingcheng Statement

Ceasing Loan from England 123

Replied to the Sichuan Shanghai Fellow Association Yesterday

According to the Guowen News Agency, the Shanghai branch of Juxingcheng received a letter of advice from the Sichuan Shanghai Fellow Association yesterday, saying that at a time when the Red disaster is serious and people are uneasy, it is not necessary for your bank to jointly establish the Lianyi Company with the British Shandeh Company, and please stop the process immediately. According to the manager of the bank, the Fellow Association received a telegram from the bank's general manager before discussing and deciding, stating that it had formally declared to the British side that it would stop the process. The original letter of reply to the Fellow Association is copied as follows: "Greetings, regarding your association's letter advising our bank to stop using foreign capital, it is because the Red disaster in Sichuan Province is serious, and the suppression of bandits is tense. Most of the funds in Sichuan Province are remitted abroad. How can we talk about investment at this moment? Your association's love for our homeland is extremely admirable, and it coincides with our bank's intention, so we should accept the cessation of the process and notify the Shandeh Company in London to cancel the draft agreement. We are concerned about your attention. This is a special reply. To the Sichuan Shanghai Fellow Association."

The Shipping Association is Concerned About Pilotage Fees

Replied to the Inspector General of Customs 124

Detailed Statement of Facts and Reasons, Requesting Instructions on Behalf of Merchants

To Avoid Forcing a Shutdown and Affecting the Overall Situation

Regarding the pilotage management committee's increase in the rate of short-term pilotage fees on the Yangtze River, the shipping industry association has appealed to the Yuan Ministry in accordance with the resolution, and declared that if forced, it will suspend navigation and wait for instructions. At the same time, it sent letters to the Inspector General of Customs, the Commissioner of Customs of the Jianghai Customs, and the Pilotage Management Committee, requesting that the new regulations be temporarily suspended until the Yuan Ministry's approval is received. It then received a reply from Acting Inspector General Luo, instructing it to persuade the shipping companies. After the association forwarded it to the companies, it again detailed the facts and reasons and instructed it to forward it to Acting Inspector General Luo, requesting that it ask for instructions on behalf of the shipping companies to avoid forcing a shutdown and affecting the overall situation. The original text of the reply is recorded as follows:

The Pilotage Management Customs are the Backbone 125

Greeting in reply, your office's letter No. 1010 was approved, instructing us to persuade all members not to oppose the newly revised pilotage fee rate, so that the matter of China's regaining pilotage rights can proceed smoothly. After forwarding it to all relevant member companies, it has been replied that the pilotage management committee is not entirely under the jurisdiction of the Customs. The shipping companies are aware of this, so they have submitted to the Yuan Ministry and requested that the fees not be increased.

However, the chairman of the committee is the Customs' maritime patrol officer. The reasons for increasing the fees are explained by the chairman, and the Customs is responsible for compulsory enforcement. It is clear that the Customs is the backbone of the committee, even if the committee is not entirely under the jurisdiction of the Customs. Moreover, the points stated by Acting Inspector General Luo are all subjective from the perspective of the pilots, which further proves that the Customs is emphasizing the pilots. Now, the statements that do not conform to the facts in the letter are stated separately below:

Chamber of Commerce Representatives Repeatedly Dissented 126

(1) Regarding the statement in the original letter that "Among the committee members, there is a representative recommended by the Shanghai Municipal Chamber of Commerce. During the meeting, it was not heard that he had any objection to the new fee rate," it was found that on May 22 this year,

The Shanghai Municipal Chamber of Commerce received a letter from Mr. Chen Tianjun (the representative of the Shanghai Municipal Chamber of Commerce), a member of the committee, stating that the revision of the pilotage fee rate was too large.

He repeatedly stated his opinion at the meeting and also sent a letter to Mr. Xi Liman, the chairman of the committee, on April 4, requesting that the original fee rate be temporarily charged. On June 22, the Municipal Chamber of Commerce again sent a proposed fee rate table based on Mr. Chen's letter,

and stated that at the meeting on June 15, the matter concerned the economy of the shipping companies, so it was necessary to solicit the opinions of the shipping companies first, and requested that the increase in the fee rate be temporarily delayed for discussion. The association also prepared opinions and sent them to the Municipal Chamber of Commerce, requesting that Mr. Chen submit them again. Therefore, not only were there early objections, but there were objections, all of which have records that can be verified. It is difficult to acknowledge that there were no objections.

High Pilot Salaries, Many Talents 127

(2) "The previous pilotage fee rate was set too low, so the monthly salary of the pilots was extremely low, sometimes only enough to pay 5 or 15 national currency units. At a time when the standard of living is increasing day by day, it seems that such a salary is not enough to maintain them, and it is necessary to make their lives stable in order to maintain specialized talents, so it is necessary to appropriately increase the salary of the pilots, and the pilotage fee rate has to be revised in order to increase revenue." The monthly salary of long-term pilots hired by various shipping companies is at least one or two hundred yuan or more, and the salary for temporary hires is even more than two or three hundred yuan per trip.

Their income is already so abundant, how can their lives not be stable? There are many pilot specialists in Songhu, so there is no need to recruit them with heavy money. At ordinary times, as soon as there is news that a ship is entering the Yangtze River, pilots with naval department licenses rush to the company to solicit pilotage work. This can prove the abundance of talents,

and also prove the abundance of salaries, so they are happy to take on the job. The statement in Acting Inspector General Luo's reply that the pilots' monthly salary is sometimes only 5 or 15 national currency units is far from the truth and makes it even more difficult for people to understand the truth.

Foreign Pilots Have Never Been Hired 128

(3) "The newly revised fee rate is slightly higher for ships with deeper drafts, but it is still less than half of the fees charged by foreign pilots in Songhu, which are almost three times higher than those of the committee, so it cannot be said to be too high." The newly revised fee rate is indeed more than doubled for ships with deeper drafts. For example, the old price for pilotage of a Chinese ship to and from Songhu once was 450 yuan in foreign currency. Now, according to the new regulations, it must be actually charged 991 yuan and 14 cents in foreign currency to and from two one-way trips, which can prove this. In the past ten years or so, Chinese ships sailing on the Shanghai-Hankou line have never hired foreign pilots, so it does not exist at all. How can it be used as a ratio? Taking a step back, if any public or private enterprise hires Chinese people and must use foreigners as a ratio, it is definitely not something that a country with insufficient public funds and a declining industry and commerce can afford. If this statement is insisted on, it will put the country's economy and the enterprise's consumption

into a desperate situation, and it is not only the shipping companies that cannot bear it.

Regaining Sovereignty Should Reduce Costs 129

(4) "The central government is actively working to regain pilotage rights." The regaining of pilotage rights is divided into two categories: (A) Foreign pilots of the Shanghai Harbor Pilotage Company. These pilots specialize in piloting postal and cargo ships of various countries from the Daji to Shanghai, and from Shanghai to the Daji. Among the dozens of them, there is only one Chinese. Not only is the fee too high, which is opposed by various foreign ships, but also the national defense is completely dismantled, which is a huge concern. The government's plan to restore this pilotage right is originally a legitimate measure, and it is also the purpose of the government to establish the pilotage management committee. Since the committee takes this as its purpose, it should actively proceed with this purpose so as not to fail the state's commission and disappoint the people's hopes. (B) Songhu Pilotage, i.e., the Yangtze River pilotage. Chinese ships do not hire foreign pilots, which has been a long-standing practice. Even foreign firms such as Taikoo and Jardine,

The long-term pilots of various liners sailing on the Yangtze River also employ Chinese people. However, when foreign ships sail to the Chinese border and enter the Yangtze River, there are still Japanese, British, and German people who are employed by the Japanese-established Yangtze River Pilotage Association and other British and German people to act as pilots. It is necessary to regain this point. However, the method should be to reduce the pilotage fee rate for Chinese people in order to abandon the other and take this. If the fee rate is increased in order to regain pilotage, it is simply going south to draw north.

Page 12

Who is Responsible for Forcing Employment? 130

Some say that the pilot is extremely important to the safety of the entire ship. Therefore, when hiring, (1) the shipowner must have absolute trust, (2) the captain

is willing to be responsible to the outside world, and (3) the insurance company that insures the ship's value must approve. If you must overstep your authority and force the shipping company to hire someone they do not want to use, then the shipowner, captain, and insurance company will naturally not be responsible for all the responsibilities and losses that occur due to the pilot's negligence. May I ask if the person who oversteps his authority and forces the employment will be held criminally liable and liable for compensation? This is especially what the companies want to understand. Acting Inspector General Luo sees that the pilots' salaries are very low and takes it as a reason for increasing the rates, which shows the virtue of taking care of the lives of technical and sanitation personnel. However, the result is that it only takes care of a few and abandons the majority, creating a deformity, making it impossible for the original personnel to seek a meager life. Not only does it lose the balance of reason, I am afraid that it runs counter to the principle of equality of the people in the republican country. This is also something that the companies cannot fathom.

Difficult to Revert if the Goal is Not Achieved 131

The rest of the reasons have been described in detail in a telegram to the Yuan Ministry.

You should ask the association to copy the draft telegram to Acting Inspector General Luo for investigation to avoid repetition. Please reply to the above and other details. The association replied that the facts stated were consistent and the reasons were sufficient. After receiving the letter, although the association has repeatedly persuaded them not to go to extremes, the companies are concerned about their own pain and the action has been decided by the public. If the goal is not achieved, I am afraid that there is no room for reversion. We are hereby attaching a copy of the telegram to the Yuan Ministry and truthfully forwarding the information. I respectfully hope that you will investigate and consult and

ask for instructions on behalf of the shipping companies to avoid forcing a shutdown and affecting the overall situation. Please reply and wait for a reply. To the Inspector General of Customs.

The Navigation Bureau's Mediation Was Successful

Baohua Ship Resumes Sailing Yesterday 132

Decision to Have the Navigation Bureau Bail Out the Shipowner

According to the Dabai News Agency, Wang Yunfa, the owner of the Baohua ship of the Pingan Shipping Company in Shanghai, was detained by the Qidong County government and has not been released. At 9:00 AM yesterday, Wang Ruqian, the representative of the Chinese Seafarers' Union, and Li Yaoting, the general manager of Pingan Company, jointly discussed solutions at the Navigation Bureau. The result of the meeting with He Daoyun, the chief of the Second Section of the Bureau, was a decision to have the Navigation Bureau bail out the Qidong County government. The Baohua ship also temporarily resumed sailing last night, awaiting a solution. If a satisfactory result is not obtained for the next shift, the entire crew of the Pingasha line will go on strike to protect the safety of all seafarers.

The Ministry of Industry Sent Li Chongdian to Shanghai

Methods for Saving the Silk and Yarn Industries 133

And Investigating the Current State of the Silk and Yarn Industries

A Meeting of Yarn Industry Groups Will Be Convened First

Our country's silk and yarn industries are affected by the dumping of foreign goods. Silk factories have almost all ceased operations, and although yarn factories are struggling to maintain operations, they are all suffering losses.

The Ministry of Industry and Commerce recently specially dispatched Section Chief Li Chongdian of the Department of Industry from Beijing to Shanghai to investigate the situation of the two industries and discuss relief measures.

The details are recorded below:

State of Decline (1) The silk industry is affected by the dumping of Japanese silk in Europe and the United States, resulting in a steady decline in the market price of Chinese silk. The price of each dan (unit of weight) of standard silk has fallen to around 400 yuan. The silk produced by silk factories is incurring heavy losses, and they have no choice but to suspend operations and wait for the opportunity. Now, almost all silk factories in Jiangsu and Zhejiang have suspended operations. In Shanghai, less than two-tenths of them are still operating. (2) The yarn industry in our country has recently been affected by the decline of the rural economy and the dumping of foreign goods, resulting in a sharp decrease in sales.

All factories have reduced their working hours to maintain operations. This year, new cotton from various places has been put on the market and it is a harvest year. Recently, sales in various places have shown improvement.

Factories that had reduced working hours have resumed one after another, but this is temporary in nature, and the spun yarn is still not profitable.

Undertaking Relief The Ministry, considering the yarn and silk industries to be the most important in our country's industry, has repeatedly convened meetings to discuss relief, but all have been suspended due to limited financial resources. This time, Section Chief Li Chongdian of the Department of Industry was specially dispatched and arrived in Shanghai a few days ago. In addition to investigating the current situation of the silk and yarn industries, he is also discussing relief measures with the Shanghai Municipal Social Bureau. This has been ongoing for days. It is reported that the Social Bureau will first invite yarn industry groups to hold a joint meeting to discuss the matter.

Municipal Government Ordered

Cooperate in Abolishing Private Postal Bureaus 135

Must Be Abolished Uniformly by the End of This Year

The Municipal Government yesterday received an order from the Executive Yuan, which stated that the Ministry of Transportation had reported that private postal bureaus in various provinces and cities were hindering the business of the postal service. Orders to abolish them had been repeatedly issued, and out of consideration, the deadline had been extended to the end of the 23rd year of the Republic (1934), and they must be abolished uniformly. This has been ordered again and again. Now that the deadline is approaching, it is feared that the private postal bureaus will use the excuse of needing time to close down and disobey orders again. In addition to ordering the Directorate General of Posts to investigate the current situation of private postal bureaus in various places and report in detail for verification, it is also appropriate to request the Executive Yuan to issue an order to the provincial and municipal governments to instruct military and political organs to effectively cooperate in the abolition, etc.

Based on this, in addition to ordering compliance and separate orders, the Municipal Government is urgently ordered to comply and instruct its subordinates to cooperate in the handling, etc. It is reported that after receiving the order, the Municipal Government yesterday issued instructions to various bureaus to cooperate in the abolition uniformly.

Beidaihe

Seaside Station Changed to Year-Round Operation 143

The Beidaihe Seaside Station of the Beining Railway, which has always opened on May 1st every year and closed in early October, is now changed to a year-round operation for the convenience of passengers. It is also scheduled to run four round-trip passenger trains between Beidaihe and Seaside Stations every day from October 1st of this year to April 30th of the following year, connecting with the train schedules of various main lines. During this period, in addition to selling various one-way and round-trip passenger tickets on this route, it will also sell first, second, and third class intermodal one-way and round-trip tour tickets at the seaside. One-way tickets will be charged at full price, and round-trip tour tickets will be charged at 75% and 85% of the ordinary one-way ticket price for two trips, respectively. However, the validity period is limited to one month from the date of issue. In addition, the road has its own hotel at the seaside, which is also open as usual during this period to facilitate travel. The above measures have been forwarded to all roads by the Intermodal Transport Department of the Ministry of Railways.

Autopsy of an Old Man Killed by a Tram 145

Zheng Zhongdao, a native of Ningbo, 79 years old, lived at No. 16, Buck Road. At about 2:00 p.m. the day before yesterday, he went out alone for something. Unexpectedly, when he passed Jing'an Temple Road and Chengdu Road, he was about to cross the road from north to south. At that time, Sun Zhilan, the driver of tram No. 83 on Route 2, was speeding from the east. He could not brake in time and knocked the old man down. Later, Chinese constable No. 2452 on duty found him and immediately copied the tram number and reported to the Xinzha Police Station by telephone, summoning an ambulance to fly the injured to Renji Hospital.

Medical treatment was ineffective, and he died soon after. After an investigation, the body was taken to the Fei Lun Road mortuary. Yesterday morning, Prosecutor Guo Wei, appointed by the First Special District Local Court, accompanied forensic doctor Zhang Yan and clerk Wang Zuji, etc., came to the mortuary to examine the body. According to Sun Zhilan, he had been driving a tram for six years. That day, Yu drove to Chengdu Road, from east to west.

Unexpectedly, the deceased suddenly came from the opposite side of the tram and crossed the road from north to south. At that time, I was driving at a figure-eight speed, and when I saw him, he was only eight or nine yards away, so Yu could not brake and knocked him down, etc. According to the witness Zhang Ting, 29 years old, from Nanxiang, living at No. 222, Rehe Road, he did not know the driver or the deceased. At that time, Yu was sitting in the car and heard the sound of braking very urgently, knowing that something had happened. Yu immediately poked his head out to see.

I saw that the deceased had been knocked to the ground by the car. The car was driving quite fast at this time, etc. According to Zheng Lindong, 23 years old, is currently studying, the deceased is my grandfather, and now that he has been crushed to death by the tram, I request that it be verified, etc.

, Mr. Guo obtained the confession and ordered the verification that the deceased Zheng Zhongdao, male, was indeed injured by tram No. 83 before his death and died. The body was handed over to his grandson Zheng Lindong to sign for coffin burial.

The record is on file. It is a critical moment for the rise and fall of the Shanghai market. We specifically telegraph you to examine and implement it. X X X X

Mr. Ye Jiaxing, Standing Committee Member of the Municipal Federation, Discusses Countermeasures to Revive the City's Economy 153

Factory Closures Resulting from Rural Bankruptcy and Sharp Decline in Purchasing Power

Unite with Fellow Businesses to Avoid Speculation

According to Xin Sheng News Agency, the Shanghai First Special District Municipal Federation of Citizens recently issued a declaration to revitalize the city's economy, advocating for measures such as a one-year postponement of industrial and commercial liquidations, interest payments as usual, and deferred rent payments. This has attracted considerable attention from the community. Mr. Ye Jiaxing, a standing committee member of the federation, expressed his views to a reporter from Xin Sheng News Agency yesterday, stating that although he had attended the recent standing committee meeting of the Municipal Federation, the agenda was to discuss the association's charter. The issue of reviving the city's economy was not formally addressed. Later, due to other matters, he left the meeting early. He deeply believes that the decline of commerce and the stagnation of the market in the country today is due to the sharp decline in the purchasing power of the people in the agricultural regions, and last year's floods in the north and droughts in the south have intensified the severity of this malady, just as a tuberculosis patient suffers from an external illness. For the present, he believes that the only solution is to make every effort to revitalize the countryside, increase the purchasing power of the people, and enable the smooth sale of various domestic products, while expanding international trade venues, in order to find a way out for foreign trade. This is the fundamental cure for revitalizing the nation's commerce. As for the sluggishness of the city's market and the decline of commerce in this municipality, in addition to the above reasons, there are other factors. One of these is the mutual infighting and destruction among businesses in the same industry. For example, in the rubber industry a few years ago, there were only seven or eight rubber factories in this city, and their business was very good and they were all profitable. However, in the last year or two, the number of rubber factories has sprung up like bamboo shoots after rain, increasing to forty or fifty. As a result, the factories are mutually suppressing each other, competing by lowering prices. There is no spirit of unity among businesses in the same industry, and they are even committing suicide. What happened to the rubber industry has also happened to other industries. No wonder the city's market is in decline. Furthermore, several large stores in this city have recently gone bankrupt. The reason for their bankruptcy is not the failure of their main business, but their involvement in businesses outside of their main business. The recent bankruptcy of the Thai Company is a clear example of this. Secondly, the managers of stores in this city often use their position as managers to engage in speculation, some are fortunate enough to create personal wealth, while the stores themselves do not benefit, and unfortunately, due to economic difficulties, they often misappropriate store funds, causing the stores to run aground or go bankrupt. Such situations are endless, and it is a cause for great lament. Therefore, I sincerely hope that the city's business community can from now on strive to unite with their fellow businesses and avoid engaging in side businesses and speculation, which will greatly help the recovery of the market. Moreover, last year, all industries had already liquidated, and it is expected that after the final settlement of the disaster relief, there will be a new and innovative undertaking. Recalling that the Civil Code drafted by the Legislative Yuan included a provision for joint and several liability of partnership stores, which was subsequently amended by the Municipal Chamber of Commerce, and a Commercial Registration Law was promised to be added to supplement it. This registration law is extremely important for newly established partnership stores. It is hoped that the legislative authorities will promulgate and implement it as soon as possible to benefit the city's commerce.
