Lunar Eclipse Tonight, Return to Fullness Tomorrow Morning 157

Total Eclipse Visible in Shanghai

According to a report from the Xujiahui Observatory, a total eclipse will be visible in Shanghai tonight and tomorrow morning. The beginning of the eclipse will be visible in Eastern Europe, Asia, Australia, the Indian Ocean, and the western part of North America. The end of the eclipse will be visible in Europe, Africa (except for the extreme western part), the Indian Ocean, Australia, the western Pacific Ocean, and the extreme northwestern part of North America. The moon will enter the penumbra at 8:39 PM this Saturday, enter the umbra at 9:03 PM, and begin to be eclipsed at 11:03 PM. The total eclipse will end at 0:31 AM on Sunday, the moon will leave the umbra at 1:41 AM, and leave the penumbra at 2:55 AM.

Declaration of the Shanghai Newspaper Industry Union 158

In 1927, when the National Revolutionary Army established itself in Shanghai and Nanjing, and the people's movement swept across the country, the newspaper workers, on the one hand, were aware of their own disunity and lack of organization, and on the other hand, felt that the National Revolution was a revolution of the entire people, and that everyone had the right and opportunity to participate in politics. Based on the above two reasons, our union was organized. Over the years, in the spirit of sincere unity of our workers and the principle of labor-management cooperation, we have strived to enhance the status of the workers themselves, improve their living conditions, and advance their work skills, in order to cultivate a spirit of self-governance, and establish workers' schools for the children of workers to have the opportunity to attend school. All these things have always been the consistent proposition of our union, and we have never forgotten them.

Since the September 18th Incident, when foreign invaders invaded and the eastern provinces were lost, the national consciousness of the people throughout the country has declined. Fortunately, the central comrades have united sincerely, maintained composure and prudence, and have a plan to deal with the national crisis: first pacify the interior, and to pacify the interior, we must first eliminate the Communist Party. The recent suppression of the communist bandits in Jiangxi, although it is due to the collapse of the communist party's own theory and its unsuitability for China, is also due to the wisdom of Chairman Chiang and the lives of the officers and soldiers, which is enough to show that our central government is becoming more stable and the national consciousness is becoming stronger, and the revival of the Chinese nation is within reach. The members of our union adhere to the Three Principles of the People, and never forget the responsibility of saving the country and the nation. We will follow the central government's intention, under the leadership of the Three Principles of the People and Chairman Chiang, and strive to fulfill the responsibility of saving the Chinese nation. Therefore, at the beginning of the 16th session of the Executive Committee of our union, we hereby declare the proposition of our union, and we hope that all sectors will understand it. This is our declaration. Shanghai Newspaper Industry Union, January 18, 1935.

The French Concession Taxpayers' Association Decided to Hold a Meeting to Discuss

The Mechanical National Goods Factory Union, based on the resolution of the second meeting of the eighth session of representatives, and the notice issued by the police department, that any organization or individual other than the French authorities is refused inspection of factories in the French Concession, which infringes on our national sovereignty, expressed their determination to oppose it to the death. Therefore, at 3:30 PM yesterday, they sent representatives Cheng Shouzhong and Gu Xiyuan to the French Concession Chinese Taxpayers' Association to petition, demanding (1) that the management regulations be temporarily suspended, and (2) that they be resubmitted for review. After arriving at the Taxpayers' Association, they were received by Chinese Committee Member Cheng Zhusun, who expressed acceptance of the two demands of the representatives and promised to convene a special meeting of all Chinese directors and committee members on Monday (21st) afternoon to discuss this matter specifically, in order to achieve the protection of sovereignty. At the same time, they also decided to submit the police department's notice to the meeting for discussion.

Yu Qiaqing Discusses How the Shanghai-Ningbo Route Issue Was Resolved 160

The Mingxing Steamer Company Will Open Scheduled Services First on Behalf of the Xinjingtian Steamer

Invitations Issued to Various Sectors to Visit on the 21st

According to Xin Sheng News Agency, the Sanbei Company acted as an agent for the Mingxing steamer to operate on the Ningbo route, including Wan Ningbo. Later, the China Merchants Steam Navigation Company and the Ning Shao Steamship Company separately sent letters to the Shanghai Maritime Affairs Bureau, requesting the bureau to suspend the issuance of the route license to the steamer. The bureau then forwarded the letters to the Sanbei Company, ordering them to respond. Later, Mr. Peng, Director of the Shanghai Maritime Affairs Bureau, invited the main personnel of the three companies to the bureau on the 12th of this month to discuss how to resolve this matter. No announcement has been made yet, and people from all walks of life are very concerned. A reporter from Xin Sheng News Agency specially visited Mr. Yu Qiaqing, General Manager of the Sanbei Company, at the company yesterday to inquire about this matter. He was received and told the following: In the afternoon of the 12th of this month, I (referring to himself) went to the bureau at the invitation of Mr. Peng, Director of the Shanghai Maritime Affairs Bureau. Those present included Mr. Liu Hongsheng, General Manager of the China Merchants Steam Navigation Company, and Mr. Yuan Fudeng, Manager of the Ning Shao Steamship Company. I then asked Director Peng whether today's meeting was to discuss the issue of suspending the issuance of the route license. Peng replied that today we have invited the three companies to discuss cooperation methods, not to suspend the issuance of the route license. I then asked the two representatives of Liu and Yuan whether they had seen the Sanbei Company's reply to the Maritime Affairs Bureau. If there were any discrepancies, they could be raised for discussion. Both representatives of Liu and Yuan acknowledged that the sections stated in the Sanbei Company's reply were factual. I then said that since you two believe that the Sanbei Company has a reason, then there is nothing inappropriate about the application. In general, the advanced shipping countries divide route licenses into three categories: ocean, coastal, and river, and there are no restrictions. There is no reason to refuse the route license based on the government's intentions. Representative Liu then said that he had tasted it with Minister Zhu, and during the preparation period for cooperation, if the Mingxing steamer insisted on sailing Shanghai-Ningbo, the route license must be suspended. I replied that it was very good. The Mingxing steamer sailing Shanghai-Zhenhai, including Wan Ningbo, was entirely for the purpose of providing relief to rural areas and facilitating transportation. I have repeatedly stated that I am willing to sacrifice the principle of making slight profits at high prices. Moreover, I do not understand which laws and regulations this violates. Does the China Merchants Steam Navigation Company have to restrict the route if it has a ship sailing on it? I am for the... even if the government considers it a violation of the order, the company will not hesitate to go bankrupt. Moreover, to take a step back, even if the Maritime Affairs Bureau approves the China Merchants Steam Navigation Company's intention and suspends the issuance of the Mingxing Shanghai-Ningbo route license, the Sanbei Company will suspend the Mingxing steamer for a long time to wait for a fair resolution. Among the route licenses of the other steamers of the Sanbei Company, there are about 20 ships with Shanghai-Ningbo routes. It is also possible to send a ship to sail. Will the Maritime Affairs Bureau cancel all of these route licenses? Director Peng then reiterated the previous remarks on cooperation. I am extremely in favor of cooperation. Moreover, the Mingxing's sailing on Shanghai-Zhenhai including Wan Ningbo completely contains the doctrine of saving the countryside, not for profit. Therefore, if it reaches the point where the tariff on the transfer of local products transported by Chinese ships is waived at the trading ports, or if the Yangtze River cooperation contract is established, the Sanbei Company can stop the Mingxing steamer from sailing to Shanghai-Zhenhai. Representative Liu then said that the Yangtze River cooperation contract could be signed in about two months. I then replied that this was not far off. I can make peaceful concessions within the scope possible without violating the doctrine of saving the countryside. Representative Liu then said that the Shanghai-Ningbo four companies could hold another meeting to discuss. I then expressed my approval and went to the China Merchants Steam Navigation Company, and invited a representative from Jardine Matheson to the bureau to discuss it together. After discussion, it was agreed that the Shanghai-Ningbo four companies' cooperation contract would continue as before. On the one hand, the China Merchants Steam Navigation Company will be responsible for signing the Yangtze River cooperation contract within two months. The Mingxing steamer will first replace the China Merchants Steam Navigation Company's Xinjingtian steamer for one month starting from the 22nd of this month. After the expiration, it will replace the Ning Shao Steamship Company's Xin Ning Shao steamer for one month. If the two-month period expires and the Yangtze River cooperation contract has not yet been finalized, the Sanbei Company will sail on its own until the day the tariff on the transfer of local goods is waived. It will be diverted to the Yangtze River. During the period of replacing the China Merchants Steam Navigation Company and the Ning Shao Steamship Company, the profits and losses will be borne by each company. The Sanbei Company will only charge ship rental, and all the crew members of each ship and the personnel of the business department, as well as the waiters in each cabin, will be handled by the personnel designated by the Sanbei Company and cannot be changed. As a solution, the Ning Shao Steamship Company's Xin Ning Shao Zhenhai will berth at the Sanbei Wharf. The reporter then asked what other important relationships you have for sailing the Shanghai-Zhenhai route, besides saving the rural areas of Shanghai. Can you tell us a few? Qing replied that in addition to saving rural areas, there are three points in sailing the Shanghai-Zhenhai route. The first point is to reduce the burden of local products. The second point is to save time for small passengers. The third point is that the Zhejiang-Jiangxi Railway is about to be completed, and goods transported from Zhejiang and Jiangxi provinces can be exported from Zhenhai. Therefore, with these three points, our company will not hesitate to sacrifice everything. The China Merchants Steam Navigation Company should not oppose this matter. It is reported that the Mingxing steamer will replace the Xinjingtian steamer on the 22nd of this month. On the morning of the day before, the Sanbei Company will invite people from all walks of life to visit the steamer at the Jinliyuan Ningbo Wharf at 11:00 AM.

Chinese and Foreign Benevolent Relief Association Reports Family of Disaster Victims in Haining Died by Poisoning 161

All Sectors Hope to Extend a Helping Hand

Wang Yusan, Ph.D. in Political Science and Sociology from [location redacted], visited the Chinese and Foreign Benevolent Relief Association on Renji Road yesterday. He told the association that near Haining, there was a family of seven, including a couple and their children. Due to the early famine, they had eaten everything and pawned everything, and had not been able to cook for three days. A neighbor, hearing this, found it difficult to sit idly by and divided several liters of rice to help them out of their immediate predicament. However, when her husband returned, he said that this little bit was not enough for them to take care of themselves, let alone give it to others. How would their family survive? The two quarreled, and their voices reached outside the house. The villager's family knew about this, so they returned the original rice. Another neighbor, learning of the situation, and that both the husband and wife were groaning, found a yuan left in the cotton wadding, though it was not used for medicine, and generously lent it to them in hopes of saving their family's lives. However, although the villager obtained this yuan, he still felt unable to survive in this environment. He suddenly had a pessimistic thought and immediately bought two jiao of broken rice and eight jiao of sodium bicarbonate, cooked porridge and took it all, resulting in the death of all seven members of the family. The tragedy spread throughout the village, and everyone was shocked. Dr. Wang also said that there are still 1,500 households in Haining that must be saved. The provincial relief is limited and slow to help. At present, the relief provided is 200 yuan per day, and it would only take 6,000 yuan to help them for a month, which can definitely save lives. It is said that the association has repeatedly increased the allocation of funds for emergency relief in Haining and has jointly distributed them with the Jisheng Association. It has only just been completed, but such a tragedy has occurred. It is a sign that the disaster is severe and the funds are meager, and it is difficult to achieve a thorough solution. If all sectors extend a helping hand, it will be a timely and supreme act of merit in this cold weather.

Jisheng Association Takes Over Emergency Relief in Haiyan 162

The Chinese Jisheng Association has completed the emergency relief in Haining and is now taking over the relief efforts in Haiyan. In this cold weather, disaster victims are everywhere, and a small amount of relief funds and clothing is difficult to popularize. There are too many monks and too little porridge, and it is inevitable that some will feel disappointed. In the blink of an eye, next spring will come, and there will be a shortage of food. Even if we only consider the nearby Jiangsu and Zhejiang provinces, the severity of the disaster areas, the number of disaster victims, the lack of food and clothing, how can they support life and spend their days? Moreover, with life hanging by a thread, how can they plant seeds in the fields and hope for spring plowing? The cries of the hungry are unbearable all day long. Those who have children who can be sold or can escape to other places are still able to save their lives. The dead are gone, and what can they say? At this time of extreme anxiety and before the ditches are filled, we hope that people in society will save the money spent on Spring Festival banquets and use it for disaster relief, so that the disaster victims will benefit greatly. This is especially what we hope for from charitable comrades.

The Moral Society Goes to Jurong to Distribute Relief 163

A Western Employee of Jardine Matheson Forced a Chinese Worker to His Death, the National Seamen's Association Provides Support 164

Tian Hou, a worker in the middle cabin of the Xianghe steamer of Jardine Matheson, had missed the ship in Shanghai and took the Longhe steamer to Beijing to catch up. He was forced to disembark at Xiaguan, and the Xianghe steamer had already set sail. He then took the Longhe steamer again. When the worker boarded the ship in Shanghai, he originally paid one yuan and one jiao to buy a half-price ticket. The second time he boarded the ship from Beijing, he could not buy a ticket because he had no money left. He was caught by a Western ticket inspector named Niumen. Despite Tian's explanation, the Westerner not only did not sympathize with a fellow seaman from the same company, but also beat him and humiliated him in every way, insisting on paying for the ticket. Tian, being forced and helpless, threw himself into the river. When they arrived in Wuhu, he was already dead. The body was collected in Wuhu, and the results of the court's examination showed that Tian had been injured before his death and drowned. The Civil Court believes there is a need for supervision

At the same time, there was also a pledge of 150,000 yuan to the Si Ming Bank, an advance payment of 150,000 yuan from the Qun Yi Banking Syndicate, and more than 100,000 yuan in deposits from relatives and friends. If the two were offset, he only owed about 500,000 yuan, so he planned to pay off half of it first, paying half to all creditors, regardless of size. Even threatened to tie them up and throw them into the sea

Kala-Azar Discovered in Jiangbei 175

Seaport Quarantine Office Prevents Spread

Health Department Sends Personnel to Diagnose and Treat

According to Dagongshe, the weather has been irregular recently, and various infectious diseases are most likely to develop. Recently, Kala-azar has suddenly been discovered in the Jiangbei area of ​​Suzhou Province, with many patients. The National Seaport Quarantine Administration, considering it a matter of public health, has recently strictly prevented its spread. The details are as follows:

Wu Liande Discusses the State of the Disease 176

According to Mr. Wu Liande, Director of the Administration, speaking to a reporter from Dagongshe yesterday, the infectious disease discovered in the Jiangbei area of ​​Suzhou Province is Kala-azar in medicine, known as (BIackFeuer) in English, which is caused by people's lack of hygiene. It starts with a slight fever, then the abdomen gradually swells, as large as a pregnant woman, resembling leprosy, and is extremely easy to spread. It is prevalent in the tropical areas of Burma and Annam. It has also been discovered in Shandong and other provinces of China, but it is not the black plague (BIackdeath) reported in the news. This administration has strictly prevented its development.

Establish clinics for treatment at any time. The Jiangbei area is mostly rural, so most of those infected with Kala-azar are farmers. The Ministry of Health believes that infectious diseases must be eradicated, so it has sent Dr. Sun Zhirong from this office to establish clinics and actively treat patients. In the shortest possible time, there may be hope for eradication. According to the current observation of the disease, it does not seem to spread excessively. There are already considerable precautions in this city.

The Tragic History of a Prostitute 178

Wandering in Shanghai with Regret

Dying of Poverty and Illness in a Foreign Land

Cao Ada, a young woman from Kunshan, aged twenty-four, has a habit of eating red pills. Recently, she has been wandering outside, lying down all day long. She was first married to Wang, who ordered her to quit the habit, but after several times of sending her to the hospital, the result was the opposite, and the addiction became even more serious than before. Wang had no choice but to divorce her. This ignorant rural woman, once deeply addicted to opium, was first not tolerated by her family, and after leaving her husband, she was dissatisfied with her destiny, and wandered alone, living under the doorway of Li Kou, ending her life in destitution, only increasing her sadness. The day before yesterday, she moved again to the entrance of Liu's Tomb in Jiumudi, lying on the ground, unable to get up due to illness, in a very miserable state. She begged passersby to write a letter for her to notify her brother-in-law to take her home. She claimed to be Cao Ada and recounted her past, deeply regretting that she had gone astray, resulting in this outcome. She asked to send a letter to Cao Yongxing's pig shop in the South City Bank of Chaoyangmen, Kunshan, to be received by her brother-in-law Cao Zaifeng. In the letter, please state that the letter is not for other matters, because my sister is wandering in a foreign land, unfamiliar with the people and place, unable to call for help. Recently, she has been seriously ill and cannot move an inch. I beg my brother-in-law to have mercy and help the fallen person, and take me back to my hometown. I will repay you greatly in the future. I am currently sick at the entrance of Liu's Tomb in Jiumudi, Shanghai. Please come quickly after seeing the letter, and take me back. If you delay, I am afraid we will not meet again. After speaking, her eyes were full of tears, regret and sadness intertwined, and she wept and recounted the situation. The onlookers were like a wall, and they all sighed with pity. Unexpectedly, yesterday morning, someone caught a glimpse of Cao Ada already dead. The incident was discovered by the Shenxiangge Police Station in the Old North Gate, which ordered the Jiumudi Bao Jia Pingyang to report to the District Court for an autopsy. In the afternoon, Prosecutor Kong Xianglin, entrusted by the court, arrived at the scene with the coroner and other personnel. After examining the body of the deceased Cao Ada (female), who was wearing old clothes and covered with sores, with emaciated muscles, it was determined that she had died of illness. A death sentence was issued, and the coffin was sealed at the funeral home, waiting for relatives to claim it. Later, a kind-hearted person asked the local Bao Jia to send a letter to Cao Zaifeng, the owner of Cao Yongxing's pig shop in Chaoyangmen, Kunshan, to come to Shanghai to claim the coffin, so that the remains could be transported back to their hometown for burial.

A secret mill was raided on Park Road

Many people are involved, and the hearing is postponed

The informant returned to report to Detective Wu, who reported to the First Special Court and signed a search warrant. On the day before yesterday, they secretly went to No. 88 Renxin Lane and waited at the entrance. At the same time, they sent an informant inside, pretending to buy, and contacted the woman Xu Yang, who told her mother, Xu Wu, to call 3247 (i.e., Yitaiyong Coal Store, No. 48 Pushi Road, French Concession) to send the goods from the mill. Before long, a Ningbo native Hu Jinsheng arrived carrying a charcoal basket. Just as he was about to enter the room, he was arrested by detectives outside the door. Ten bags of red pills were found in the coal, weighing five and a half pounds, and the two women were arrested and searched. No prohibited items were found. Then, according to Hu's confession, they went with detectives from the French Police Station to the Yitaiyong Coal Store and found 26 pounds of red pills, three taels of powder, two pounds of coffee essence, one batch board of red pills, and two tins of red pill pigment on top of the firewood. At that time, only one Ningbo woman, Zhang Wang, was arrested. Later, Hu Jinsheng confessed that the red pills were obtained from the Shidai Pharmacy at No. 21 Jinshou Lane, Shandong Road. Chinese and Western detectives went to the Shidai Pharmacy and arrested accomplices Zhang Zinan, a Ningbo native, and his brother Zhang Ziqing (formerly a doctor). Sixteen pounds of raw materials, five bottles of rubber, weighing five and a half pounds, and five tins of coffee acid were found under the bed in the back room and taken to the police station and detained separately. Yesterday morning, they were sent to the Criminal Eighth Court of the First Special Court. Lawyer Zhang Tianyin of the police station stood up and stated the case, and said that the trademark of the red pills seized in this case was Shuangshi Horse Brand, and it was also marked with English letters, saying that the goods were excellent and manufactured in Germany. It was also found that the person in charge was Liu Chongfa, the manager of Yitaiyong Coal Store, who is now at large. Therefore, he requested permission to detain the defendants and postpone the trial. Judge Liu Yugui briefly interrogated Xu Yang and the other six people. Their confessions mostly evaded responsibility. He then ordered that they be detained for seven days for further interrogation.

Zhang Guanghua Denies Killing His Younger Brother 181

The trial opened yesterday to take statements

The case needs further study

Zhang Guanghua, a Henan native who previously worked in the Shanghai Navigation Administration Bureau, aged 27, and his 18-year-old younger brother Zhang Guangzhou lived together in the three-story pavilion room of Ningbo woman Dai Chen's house at No. 24 Chongde Lane, Minguo Road, outside the Xiaobeimen of the French Concession. On November 22 of last year, Zhang Guanghua's job was terminated, so he resigned from the house to the sub-landlord, planning to return to Henan with his brother in five or six days. That night, the two brothers still slept in the same room. At 5:00 am the next morning, Zhang Guangzhou was suddenly killed by a knife cut to the neck. At the same time, Zhang Guanghua also suffered five or six knife wounds to the head, jumped out of the window and shouted for help, and called to open the door and windows of the two-story pavilion room, where Haiyan native Yan Jintao lived. The relatives of the sub-landlord, Dan Bingchang and Lin Shengxiang, went out to report to the police station, and Guanghua was sent to the hospital for treatment. At the same time, Guangzhou's body was taken to the coroner's office to request the Second Special Court to send someone to verify it. Since there were no relatives in Shanghai, the body was buried by the charity hall. Later, Guanghua recovered from his injuries and was brought back by the police station for strict investigation. It was determined that Guangzhou was indeed killed by Guanghua, and Guanghua was sent to the Second Special Court for public prosecution on charges of murder. On the 8th of this month, Judge Xiong Huiping held a trial and interrogated the witnesses Dai Chen, Yan Jintao, Dan Bingchang, Lin Shengxiang, etc., and then issued an order to postpone the retrial. The details have been reported in detail in the Japanese newspaper. During the postponement, the presiding judge Xiong personally went to the scene of the incident to investigate and inquire about the events at the time. Yesterday was the date of the continued trial. Judge Xiong and clerk Tao opened the Criminal Second Court to hear the case again. Lawyer Yuan Jiahong of the Police Department appeared in court, and the defendant Zhang Guanghua also hired a lawyer to defend him. The defendant's father Zhang Wenfu also came to court to listen. According to Zhang Guanghua, our brothers have always had a good relationship. Q: Why did such a tragedy happen? A: I was injured and escaped. I don't know that I turned off the lights and went to sleep at night. Someone used a knife to cut my head in my sleep. I woke up and got up, but I couldn't open the door, so I jumped out of the window and shouted for help. This person also cut my younger brother. Q: Did your younger brother cut you? A: There was no light, so I couldn't see clearly. I was sleeping on the bed by the east window, with my feet facing the door, and my head covered with a blanket. My right shoulder was down and my left shoulder was up. At this point, the witnesses were interrogated one by one. Their statements were the same as those reported earlier. The official then said to the defendant, now it is proved that there was no third person in your room. According to various observations, it is presumed that your brother cut you, and you fought back, which is reasonable. And you admitted this when you were moving out. Zhang replied, our brothers have always been harmonious, and he is very obedient to me. If he didn't obey me, I could have asked him to live elsewhere. How could I have harmed my own brother? At this point, the official said that the case still needed detailed study, and ordered the clerk to read the transcripts of the statements of each person, sign them, and then ordered that the case be postponed for further interrogation. The defendant was still remanded in custody.

Zhu Liqing Case Opened in Execution Court Yesterday 182

Le Songxiong Has Not Yet Paid Alimony

The court will schedule another subpoena

Zhu Liqing, a girl from Nanjing, lives at No. 30 Datong Lane, Yaozhu Road, French Concession. She received higher education and is proficient in both Chinese and Western languages. In the spring of 1919 of the Republic, she was hired by Le Zhenbao, a Ningbo native who owns the Taichang Wood Shop on Nanjing Road, as an English teacher. At that time, Le Zisongxiong, who was the film department buyer of the Pacific Fair, saw that Zhu was talented and beautiful, and couldn't help but desire her. He pursued Zhu in every way. In 1919, he invited Zhu to visit the famous scenic spots in Hangzhou and had an ambiguous relationship. In April of the following year, Zhu gave birth to a daughter, named Zhi'er by Songxiong. At the same time, Songxiong and Zhu rented a house at No. 598 Laoshenfu Road and lived together. By October 1921, Zhu gave birth to another daughter, named Ren'er. Since Zhu and Le lived together, their relationship was very harmonious, and she was very happy that she would be with him for the rest of her life. Unexpectedly, the beautiful scene did not last long. Since last autumn, Le suddenly changed his attitude towards Zhu, treating her like an old fan. Zhu had no choice but to hire lawyer Xue Jiaqi to file a complaint with the Civil Court of the Second Special Court, requesting that the defendant Le Songxiong be ordered to pay living expenses of 12,000 yuan and return the advance payment of 1,500 yuan. Judge Ma Yishu heard the case several times. The defendant Le Songxiong also hired lawyer Yan Yinwu to represent him in court, and filed a counterclaim, requesting that the court order a separation from Zhu and hand over the two daughters to Le for support. The case has been decided, ordering the defendant Le Songxiong to pay the plaintiff Zhu Liqing alimony of 6,000 yuan, return the advance payment, and pay monthly living expenses of 60 yuan during the appeal period. The defendant's lawsuit was dismissed. However, the defendant has not yet paid. Yesterday morning was the civil enforcement period, and Judge Shu issued a subpoena to both parties for enforcement. As for the 120 yuan for two months' living expenses during the appeal period, as only Miss Zhu attended the court, Judge Shu宜諭instructed that the defendant's subpoena had not been delivered and would be resubpoenaed on a scheduled date.

Since You've Called Him Son-in-Law, There's No Need to Abandon Friendship and Promote Hatred 183

Marriage Disputes Involve Lawsuits in Court

The judge's intention is best to reconcile

Gu Wenzhong, a local, is in the customs declaration business. His home is on Zhonghua Road, Nanshi.

Social Bureau Sends Letter to Shelter for the Poor to Fill Out Vagrant Interview Records 184

Zhang Zixin, Director of the Shelter for the Poor, sent a letter to the administrators, ordering them to investigate the situation of the poor and fill out the interview records, so as to submit them to the Social Bureau. The letter reads: I am writing to inform you that the Social Bureau has issued a letter stating that the vagrant interview records have been printed by this Bureau. We are now sending 1,450 copies. Please fill them out in detail, item by item. If there are not enough, you can ask adults to fill them out. As for those under the age of sixteen, you can use another type to fill them out. Enclosed is a sample sheet. Please print and handle it. Check the said vagrant interview records, the Social Bureau has been handling the matter for investigation and statistics for previous sessions, and now specially send 500 copies, and another type of sample sheet, printed and sent 100 copies, hope you will follow and handle them, and fill them out in detail, in order to compile and forward them for your consideration.

Shanghai Municipal Social Bureau Vagrant Interview Record, what is your surname, what is your name, how old are you, where are you from, who are the people in your family, where are they now, what are they doing, can you read, have you been to school, what skills do you have, how long have you been in Shanghai, how did you come, what did you do when you first came to Shanghai, what do you do in Shanghai, how do you make a living, have you ever sent money home when you worked in Shanghai, do you often send it, do you have any illnesses, when did you get to this point, why did you come here, are you willing, why, have you ever gambled, do you often gamble lately, do you drink alcohol, how much can you drink, what kind of alcohol do you drink, do you have cigarettes (opium morphine), no, do you have red pills, no, among the prostitutes, can you name one or two, what is your relationship with them, have you ever been sued, what crime did you commit, are you willing to correct your mistakes, how do you plan to correct them, where do you plan to go after you leave the shelter, what do you plan to do,

Last year, he formed an indissoluble bond with Gu Yizhen, a woman from the countryside of Wuxi. Gu is only eighteen years old and unmarried. Her elder sister, Sai Zhen, lives in Jiumudi in the city. Since Gu started living with Yizhen, he initially agreed to marry her as his wife, so Yizhen's mother, Bao, and Sai Zhen both agreed. Bao always addressed Gu as "son-in-law" in her letters to Gu and regarded herself as the mother-in-law. The letters were mostly forwarded through Sai Zhen's place to avoid mistakes. Unexpectedly, Gu Wenzhong has recently become ungrateful and treats Yizhen as a stranger. Her mother, Gu Bao, in the name of her daughter's legal guardian, hired a lawyer to sue Gu Wenzhong for interfering with the family in the First Special District Court, requesting legal punishment. Judge Wu Tingqi has held court hearings several times. Since Gu Bao has already recognized Gu Wenzhong as her son-in-law, he advised both parties to reconcile out of court, and there is no need to abandon friendship and promote hatred. However, although both parties appreciated the judge's intention to settle the matter, they were still unwilling to negotiate openly and reconcile. Half a month has passed and it has not yet been resolved. Yesterday afternoon, the court hearing was held again. The defendant Gu Wenzhong did not attend, but the plaintiff Gu Yizhen attended with her lawyer, requesting another extension so that they could continue to negotiate. Judge Wu granted the request and postponed the retrial to 1:25 pm next month. If a settlement has been reached before the next court hearing, they should submit a written request to withdraw the complaint.

Zhabei Soup Kitchen Hosts Press Visit 185

The Zhabei Liuying Road soup kitchen hosted members of the city's press corps for a visit yesterday morning. Around 8:00 AM, over ten reporters from various newspapers gathered at the Guanshengyuan on Nanjing Road, had a quick breakfast, and set off. They arrived at the kitchen on Liuying Road around 9:00 AM. Subsequently, they were led on a tour by Wang Bin-yan and others. The tour concluded around 10:00 AM, and the kitchen provided transportation back. Details are as follows:

Over 20,000 People Await Food　When the reporters arrived at Liuying Road, the soup distribution had just finished. A crowd of impoverished people, men, women, old, and young, in tattered clothes, carrying ladles and basins, poured out from the soup kitchen. In this beautiful city, who would have expected so many refugees, desperately waiting for food, numbering over 20,000. Their faces were filled with sorrow, a truly unbearable sight. The reporters then disembarked and were greeted by Mr. Wang Bin-yan and others, who led them inside for a tour.

Copper Coins Given to Those Who Didn't Get Soup　Inside were three temporary sheds, made of coarse bamboo with dense grids, intended as resting places. One was for men, one for women, and one for children, to prevent crowding during distribution and to protect women and children from being squeezed. Each shed had its own entrance for separate exits in batches. Security guards were stationed to maintain order. There were also five thatched huts, each with two stoves, and each stove had three pots, along with a total of seventeen large vats. Based on the soup distribution that morning, approximately 40 dan (a Chinese unit of dry volume, about 50 kg) of rice were cooked. Those who couldn't get soup were given copper coins, totaling 53 yuan. The cooking of the soup began at 11:00 PM, and the soup was stored in the vats, each vat able to serve 300 people. The doors were opened at 4:00 AM, and people went to the distribution room to receive soup. Adults received three ladles each, and children received two. After receiving the soup, they went to the temporary sheds. The doors were closed around 8:00 AM and opened again around 9:00 AM for people to leave in batches.

Wang Bin-yan Speaks of the Plight of the Poor　Mr. Wang also told the Central News Agency reporter that the number of poor people between Zhabei and Jiangwan who came here for food due to hunger and cold reached tens of thousands daily, of whom over 7,000 were men, and two-thirds were young and strong. These were mostly unemployed workers or laborers. Many factories in Zhabei were closing, and the commercial situation was even more dismal. Even rickshaw pulling could not guarantee a full meal. Furthermore, what is particularly noteworthy is that in previous years, those who came to the soup kitchen were mostly people from Jiangbei or Anhui, with very few locals. Now, there are many locals, even from as far as Jiangwan, who braved the elements and trekked long distances at 2:00 AM, hoping for a bowl of soup. Also, because of the large number of people, the soup kitchen had to distribute soup to everyone, but what one person received could not support the whole family. Therefore, the old, the young, and the sick had to be helped along the way. The people of Shanghai and various charitable organizations know about the disasters in other provinces and call for relief, but they do not observe the suffering of the lower classes in Shanghai, which is no less than that of the disaster victims in other provinces. This is regrettable. He hopes that the gentlemen of the press will publicize this in the newspapers so that all sectors can understand the truth and provide substantial assistance.

Effective from February 1st of this Year

Regarding the proposal to issue round-trip tourist tickets from Pukou Station on the Jinpu (Tianjin-Pukou) Railway to various stations on the Jinghu (Beijing-Shanghai) and Huhangyong (Shanghai-Hangzhou-Ningbo) Railways, it was resolved at the 17th National Joint Transportation Conference and approved by the Ministry of Railways. Death Caused by Falling Cargo 192

Yu Qiaqing Offers 500 Yuan in Compensation to the Deceased's Family

Fan, the Comprador, Generously Donates to Transport the Coffin Back to Tianjin

Regarding the incident on December 28th last year, in which a man from Tianjin named Huang Xiufeng was killed on the Sanbei Company's Jing'an Steamer when a cargo of corn collapsed in the cargo hold during a trip to Shanghai to visit his son, as reported in previous issues, it has been learned that Huang's wife, Huang Anshi, rushed here from Tianjin upon hearing the news, weeping loudly over the coffin. She expressed that after Huang's tragic death, she did not know who would be able to support their family of nine, and that the eldest son was still in school, the second son was young, and the four daughters were waiting to be married. In order to maintain their future livelihood, she and her eldest son, Guisheng, went to the Sanbei Company on Guangdong Road to meet with General Manager Yu Qiaqing to express their hardship and request compensation. Huang Guisheng also reported to the 8th Branch of the Second Special District Municipal Federation for assistance, which resolved to forward the matter to the Second Special District Municipal Federation. It was resolved to request Mr. Yu Qiaqing to provide generous compensation, and Director Wu Guowei was sent with a letter to meet with Mr. Yu Qiaqing, who relayed the plight of the deceased's family. Mr. Yu Qiaqing was deeply sympathetic and approved a special compensation of 500 yuan. At the same time, Mr. Fan Menglin, the comprador of the Jing'an Steamer, also acted righteously, generously donating money to help the deceased's family transport Huang Xiufeng's coffin back to Tianjin, to avoid further burdening the family. Mother and son Huang Anshi were deeply grateful, and on the morning of the day, they filed a statement with the District Court Prosecutor's Office to collect the coffin and close the case. They then sealed the coffin for transport and went to the Sanbei Company to collect the compensation before returning to Tianjin that day.

A Petty Theft of Rice Causes a Disturbance 194

Yesterday morning, the Zhaoxing Steamer arrived at the British-owned Longmao Wharf in Lujiazui, Pudong. At 11:00 AM, while the rice was being unloaded, a porter from Shandong named Ma Keli secretly stole some loose rice, hiding it around his waist, intending to leave the wharf. He was discovered by Li Buyue, a police officer stationed at the wharf, who went forward to search him. However, Ma immediately dumped the stolen rice into the Huangpu River, so that no stolen goods were found. Feeling justified, he argued with Officer Li. The officer then blew his whistle, and officers from nearby posts came to assist in detaining Ma for questioning. After a while, another porter, Zhang Xueyin, gathered dozens of fellow workers and crowded at the entrance of the station, demanding Ma's release. The workers were all carrying carrying poles, iron hooks, and other items. Unable to achieve their demands, they took the opportunity to smash the windows of the station and injured Officer Li Buyue's left hand and left face. Another officer, Kong Xiangxi, also had the back of his left hand injured and bleeding. They also tore the pocket of his uniform. Zhang Baiyi, the comprador of the wharf, was informed of the incident and immediately telephoned the Pudong Public Security Branch Bureau. Director Zhang of the branch bureau ordered Police Chief Guo Yongliang to rush to the scene to suppress the situation. Fortunately, no major incident occurred. The troublemaking workers, Ma Chongli and Zhang Xueyin, as well as the foreman Wei Rixin, were taken to the bureau for questioning, and the two injured officers were sent to the Pudong Hospital for treatment. At this time, the Shandong workers stopped working to show their support. The branch bureau sent police for the second time to suppress the situation, and the workers continued to work. Afterwards, the branch bureau director sent the three arrested persons to the headquarters for further action. In the afternoon, the wharf comprador sent a letter to the branch bureau, detailing that the workers had been in dispute over wages for adding two or three floors to the warehouse, and this time they used this as a pretext to cause trouble. He requested continued police protection to avoid a strike.

Worker Injured in House Demolition 195

The two buildings at No. 46 and No. 48 Xinxing Road, West of the Han Bridge in Zhabei, had previously suffered a major fire. Although there were no major losses, the wood and tiles were no longer usable. The landlord ordered a construction company to demolish and rebuild them. Yesterday afternoon, around 3:00 PM, six or seven workers were climbing on the roof, dismantling the roof tiles, when the roof beam, which had been charred by the fire, could not bear the weight and broke. All the workers fell down. Fortunately, the height was not high, and they only suffered minor injuries. An ambulance was called and they were sent to the Second Hospital of the Red Cross for treatment.

Compilation of New Book Records from Shenbao Circulating Library Published 200

Price: 200 Cash per Volume

Add 7 Cents Postage for Mail Orders

The Shenbao Circulating Library (3rd Floor, Continental Shopping Arcade, Nanjing Road) has been in operation for two years. It provides various books for free reading and has established a foreign borrowing system. It has been very successful. To date, the number of readers in Shanghai and other places has exceeded 10,000. In order to facilitate readers, the library has always compiled a catalog. However, because new books are purchased every month, the catalog is also printed on time. At the end of the year, the past catalogs are re-edited and compiled into one volume. It is learned that the library's book catalog compilation for this year has now been published, containing 30,000 books. It also includes various regulations of the library, as well as the "Reading Guidance" regulations, which were created last year to answer readers' questions about books, all in one thick volume. The price is 200 cash per volume. Add 7 cents postage for mail orders (for Shanghai and other places). The library's borrowing regulations will be sent immediately upon request.

Two New Rubbings Released by the Medical Bookstore 202

"Rubbing of Lv Yaoxian's Xiao Jian Si Zhu Coin," one volume. This is a rubbing of the Xiao Jian Si Zhu coin, presented by Minister Lv Yaoxian to Mr. Chen Shouqing. There are as many as 54 types. Bao Zinian's "Explanation of Coins" says, "Xiao Jian Si Zhu, one side has the leaf pattern, one side is small Seal Script." It is the most difficult to obtain. The saying among coin collectors is that one coin in the capital is worth 20,000 to 30,000 cash. At the end of the Daoguang reign, a pot suddenly appeared in the South, and Yaoxian obtained hundreds of them, which he distributed. Not only are the sizes different, but some are upside down, some read left to right, and some have one character upright and one character upside down. Some are placed horizontally on the top and bottom of the square hole, some are facing left and right, some are upside down, some have rubbed shapes, and there are four stars, four circles, and four broken patterns. The Xiao Jian coin has the difference of both sides being the same text or being inverted or horizontally placed, and rubbed shapes. The Si Zhu coin also has both sides being the same text, and the characters also written above and below the square hole. All kinds of peculiarities, up to 54 kinds. Although it is as small as an elm pod, the bluish-green color penetrates to the bone and is absolutely precious to play with. Coins become more and more peculiar, and are fully prepared by our dynasty. It is believed that the land does not hide treasures." Now, comparing this rubbing with Bao's description, everything is in agreement. It is truly a grand sight of Xiao Jian Si Zhu coins. Now it is printed with a glass plate, and it is no different from the real rubbing. The actual price is one yuan per volume.

"Rubbing of Chen Shouqing's Six Coins and Ten Cloth Coins," one volume. This is a rubbing presented by Mr. Chen Shouqing to Minister Wu Qingqing. It first lists Wang Mang's Spring Coins and Ten Cloth Coins. The Ten Cloth Coins have two sets: one with a small straight line above the square hole, and one without it. At the end, there are rubbings of ancient coins such as Force Cloth. Now, it is printed with Chen's original version, which is no different from the real rubbing, seeing it is like seeing the real coin. The actual price is one yuan per volume. General Distributor: Medical Bookstore, No. 204 Meibai Road, Shanghai.

Fruit Row Clerks Organize a Fellowship Association 203

The fruit row clerks, in view of the oppression they have suffered from the owners in recent years, using their sweat and blood to earn meager wages like oxen and horses, repeatedly being deducted by the owners, and for the purpose of increasing the knowledge and skills of the clerks and improving their lives, felt the necessity to organize a group. Therefore, dozens of clerks initiated and jointly submitted a request to the Municipal Party Department to organize the Shanghai Fruit Industry Trade Union. The organization was approved, and Rong Baokang, Hong Dexing, Shen Baokun, Xu Binggui, Bao Liren, Chu Songhai, Weng Wuquan, Jiang Wenquan, Zheng Wensong, and other nine people were appointed as preparatory members. At the beginning of the registration, Cai Runshan, chairman of the Fruit and Ground Cargo Industry Association, repeatedly ordered the clerks to sign, provide willingness statements and surety bonds, citing violations of Articles 31 and 32 of the Trade Union Law, in order to disrupt the organization, almost leading to a major dispute. After mediation, in order to resolve the matter peacefully, the labor side complied with the mediator's intentions and changed the name of the Shanghai Fruit Industry Trade Union to the Shanghai Fruit Industry Clerks' Fellowship Association. The change was approved by the Municipal Party Department. The clerks held a meeting to discuss and decided to continue to entrust Rong Baokang and the other nine people to be responsible for the preparations. It is heard that the association will soon complete the preparations and set a date to hold a general meeting to elect directors and supervisors, to see its success.

Special Article

Peng Xiangying Lectures on the Relationship Between Citizens and Air Defense (Continued) 209

However, when we should make efforts, all the sand and fire extinguishers used to extinguish fires caused by incendiary bombs, as well as buckets and other items used for fire prevention, we must fully prepare them in peacetime, and within the possible range, we must also purchase gas masks, so that when enemy planes drop incendiary bombs and gas bombs at the same time during wartime, we can engage in firefighting work.

However, in wartime, if an incendiary bomb falls, it must be immediately covered with sand to extinguish it and prevent it from spreading. If it has spread and affected other objects, fire extinguishers or buckets of water should be used to extinguish it. Even residents in neighboring lanes must immediately gather and work together to rescue. In addition, government offices, schools, factories, and major companies should always have fire-fighting equipment, and organize employees, workers, and students into fire brigades for pre-training. Then, with wartime preparations, if peacetime disasters occur, the benefits of fire-fighting can be obtained.

The above is specifically about the importance of the responsibilities borne by citizens in terms of fire prevention. During air raids, all duties such as poison prevention, rescue, construction, security, traffic management, and alarm transmission also require citizens to take the lead, because these are the tasks most closely related to citizens. If citizens do not take the initiative to take on these tasks, even if the government leads, it will not be easy to achieve thorough and widespread results. Therefore, the relationship between citizens and air defense is indeed extremely close, and the task of air defense is indeed entirely up to the citizens.

Recently, our government authorities, feeling the frequent national crises and the pressing dangers, and the ambition of strong neighbors still growing, in case of an emergency, our important cities will inevitably be raided and turned to ashes in an instant. Therefore, in November of last year, the first air defense exercise was held in the capital, which can be said to be a guide in the national air defense facilities. Because this air defense exercise not only gave the citizens of Nanjing a very deep understanding of air defense, but also made the people across the country feel the need for air defense. If we already have a considerable understanding of air defense and know that it is an urgent and serious problem, we should actively study it and strive to implement it. Although our country lacks financial resources and lags behind in everything, the necessary national defense construction cannot be done all at once, but as long as all our comrades can embrace the determination to work hard, it will not be difficult to catch up and keep pace with the great powers. (The End)

The Eighth Episode of "Little Xitian" by Zhang Henshui 210

A Petty Official in a Remote Place Comes with a Strong Order

In a Magnificent Hall, There Are Pitiful Insects Outside

On Cheng Zhiqian's side, he knew very well that Zhang and Li were both vulgar official insects, but since they were greeting him politely, he was too embarrassed to ignore them. So when Zhang Jiefu came with that flattering attitude, he had no choice but to greet him with a smile and ask him to sit down. However, he had his own way of doing things, so he reached into his arms and groped for a while. He took out a small blue cloth package, opened it, and inside was a white silk handkerchief. Opening the white silk handkerchief, there was a red paper tray, holding two pieces of jade ware. One was a finger ring with a half-circle edge, and the other was a finely carved small jade horse. Cheng Zhiqian was a little surprised. Could it be that he was also in the jade business and came to solicit business? Zhang Jiefu smiled and held the red paper tray with both hands. He handed it to Cheng Zhiqian and said, "This little thing is just a token of my respect." Cheng Zhiqian was even more stunned. They had no friendship with each other. Why would he send such valuable gifts? How could he dare to accept them? He shook his hands repeatedly and said, "I dare not, I dare not. How can I receive such a great favor?" Zhang Jiefu placed the jade on the table, cupped his hands and said, "I also know that Mr. Cheng is unwilling to give me face. But if I explain, Mr. Cheng can accept it. I have a fellow villager in the city of Xi'an who is in the antique business. I went to see him today, and he casually gave me these two things. The things he gave me were not without meaning. He thought that I knew many people in the political world and that someone would come to Xi'an to buy antiques. He asked me to introduce one or two. I think it would be a waste if he gave these things to me. Moreover, they are worth thirty or forty yuan. It is really inconvenient for me to use. Mr. Cheng is a person with wide contacts. It is said that a precious sword is given to a hero, so I will give it to Mr. Cheng." (Eleven

Six)

The Face of a Great Man (Tian Sheweng) 211

After reading Mr. Jiangniao's "Four Strange Faces," which said that famous people in Shanghai all have strange faces, I was reminded of the faces of the great men of the Party and the country. Here are a few examples: (1) The face of a scholar-official: Wang Jingwei, President of the Executive Yuan, is known to all as a revolutionary pioneer and a great contemporary politician. Now in his fifties, he looks like a Confucian scholar, only about forty years old:

Spring and Autumn Anecdotes 212

Xi Shi is a typical beauty in Chinese history. Her hometown is Zhuji's Luoluo Village in Zhejiang. It is said that a supremely beautiful woman is still born in that village every year, but she is always unfortunate and dies young.

Zheng Banqiao said: "We scholars, holding a book, want to become officials, how to seize money, build big houses, and acquire more property; from the beginning, we went the wrong way, and later it became worse and worse, and there was no good result." But how many scholars in the world do not follow this path? (Banana Heart)

This is the same as Mr. Hu Hanmin. They are both gentle white-faced scholars. Where can you see that they are great revolutionary men? History says that Zhang Zifang looked like a woman. You know it's not a mistake.

(2) The face of a bodhisattva: Mr. Dai Jitao, President of the Examination Yuan, used to read his essays in the Tianduo Bao and Minquan Bao. They were sharp and sharp, and I imagined what kind of person he was. Since converting to Buddhism, he has been solemn and compassionate, overflowing with eyebrows, really like the "wonderful appearance of the Tathagata" of Mr. Wang Yiting, Wang Xiaolai, and Di Pingzi in Shanghai.

(3) The face of an immortal: Mr. Chu Minyi, Secretary-General of the Executive Yuan, is tall and extraordinary. He is proficient in Tai Chi. He looks like one of the Eight Immortals. This may be because learning changes temperament and appearance.

(4) The face of an old woman: Mr. Wu Zhihui, a member of the Central Committee who calls himself the old woman Liu in the Daguan enclosure, is old and has a pursed mouth, which is a bit like the "face of an old woman." However, although Mr. Wu's mouth is pursed, his tongue is like a lotus flower. When he opens his mouth, he is extremely humorous and profound. He is truly worthy of being the old woman Liu.

The Decline of Handicrafts (Chen Liang) 213

From the mouths of several fellow villagers who are craftsmen, I learned about the recent decline of handicrafts. Although they are still lucky enough not to be unemployed, they can only make a living, and their lives are extremely difficult. Their short shirts and pants are worn into the color of soy sauce. They don't even have money to get a haircut or take a bath. Now I will write down the words of a few people below, which is also a serious social problem.

A tailor said: "People think that clothes can't always be saved. It's true, but in this year, the market is not good, and money is not easy to earn. Ordinary people's daily expenses are all tightening their belts. For example, old styles are turned over, big ones are changed to small ones, and leather ones are replaced with a new face. It's over. New clothes can be saved if they can be saved. In this way, we tailors have no future. The table is deserted, and the tailors are frowning and playing five passes. Do you think it's still doing well?"

A book cover maker said: "Friends who read books know that now all books have been changed to hardcover and Western-style books. Some time ago, there were still some thread-bound books that used book covers. Now, they have been affected by the competition and dumping of bookstores, and many ancient books and old novels have been reprinted as single books, with Western paper covers. They think that book covers are outdated and superfluous. The people who make book covers have also been deprived of their jobs."

[P Street fragrance floats princess original thin drive translation

This is another section of extremely hard-won professional knowledge. All the countless lines of sight are focused on that Semar, which has been covered in dust for a long time and has only been hastily cleaned today, and the Empress Dowager is particularly complacent.

Comparing this hard and brave life of the former people with the life in the palace now, I really don’t know how much difference there is! It almost makes us unable to believe that the former rulers of Manchuria could really endure such hardship and struggle! In fact, some are not fake! Not only the leader, but all the royal relatives, ministers and attendants in the palace can be said to be tempered and polished in this kind of life every day: at this moment, hundreds of years of luxurious Chinese life have completely softened us.

At that time, we had visited all the three small palaces. Then, under the leadership of the Empress Dowager, we walked to the square outside. In the past, almost every day someone used his courage and strength to fight with those beasts with sharp claws on this square. Now, it has become a useless wasteland, but the forest on the west side of the field is more lush and lush. The tall shadows of the trees are shaking on the ground, almost making us suspect that some wild beasts will rush out of it. The Empress Dowager raised her head and looked around casually, as if she sighed with great emotion.

Before we decided to come here, the Empress Dowager had said something about the approximate history of this day's commemoration in the Shengjing Palace, and also allowed us to tell us the details after seeing a forest here: Now. We have already arrived in front of this forest, so her appointment has also been fulfilled! (Two hundred and twenty-six)

A mahogany maker said: "We rely on our strength to make a living. As long as we can pull a saw for a day, we don't have to worry about being hungry. However, the current generation is all about Western style. They use Western-style woodenware. The wealthier ones don't even use anything from the toilet to the chrome bed. Moreover, small pieces are not available in Western stores. Now that we have strength but no work, is it our dead end?"

There are also grinding, copper making ...... I can't write much. In short, some people in the city who have the ability to buy are worshipping Europe. All daily necessities are imported, even the toilet paper used in the toilet is not made in China. As for the inland, all the clothing and utensils that were originally available have to be sent to the pawnshop to pawn money. What purchasing power can we talk about? The result of the above is that China's national industry is declining, and the handicraft industry is collapsing behind the machine-made industry.

The Mad Dance of Skeletons: Black Fever Bacteria in Jiangbei

Taste (Yan Xunlou) 214

Food has various tastes, and the ability to distinguish these tastes depends entirely on the mouth.

The mouth can taste what is sweet, what is salty, what is sour, what is bitter, and what is spicy.

People's tastes also vary. Generally speaking, the largest number of people like to eat sweet things, followed by those who like to eat salty things, and then those who like to eat sour and spicy things. As for those who like to eat bitter things, it can be said that there are very few.

My second brother loves to eat sour things. Every time he eats noodles, he always complains that the soup is too salty. Once, the family deliberately put only vinegar in his noodle soup. After he finished eating, they asked him how the soup tasted. He said, "The soup tastes very good today, but it's a little less salty." In fact, he didn't know that there was no salt in the soup at all! This is also a joke about taste.

A cook who wants to please his master seems to have to know his master's taste first, but this cannot be considered a good cook. A really good cook is able to cook delicious dishes that everyone who eats can accommodate and adapt to his taste.

Therefore, we ask that all cooks be able to cook standard and compelling delicacies: at the same time, we also hope that all people who eat have standard and tasteful tongues.

Where the Traveler's Footsteps Reach

Night Visit to Tianning Temple (Fire and Snow Bright) 215

The flourishing of Chinese Buddhism has a long history, and there are many ancient monasteries and temples throughout the land that have long been famous. Just taking Tianning Temple as an example, there are already four locations: one outside Xihuan, Beiping; one outside Tianning Gate in Jiangdu; one outside the West Gate of Haikang County in Guangdong; but the one I am talking about is that one built during the Tang Dynasty outside the East Gate of Changzhou City.

Traveling to Changzhou, it was an overcast day in early winter without snow. Walking into the train station, looking at the distant city center, it was already dotted with bright lights. The night wind was blowing very strongly. I hailed a rickshaw and went into the city alone, planning to drink my fill of Lanlu famous wine and devour some thin-skinned, fresh pork, because it was my first visit and I let the rickshaw pull me wherever it went. I could say I was completely ignorant of the names of the streets we passed. However, judging from the city's appearance, where commerce wasn't very developed at night, it was still similar to Guicheng in Yixing.

The rickshaw was stopped at Xiaofu Bridge. Fortunately, the lights were burning brightly in the night market. Turning towards the west side of the bridge, I glimpsed Deshun Restaurant on Xianzhi Street. I was feeling quite hungry, so I went upstairs to "repair my five internal organs." Needless to say, the taste of the wine didn't compare to Dongpu Xingruan Society of Shaoxing. Li Taibai's "Lanling fine wine, amber-colored fragrant" was just an occasional expression of exuberance. However, the Dongpo fatty pork was no less delicious than that of Huangzhou, Hubei. I especially loved the sugar-soaked celery, which was excellent in both color and flavor!

After eating and drinking to my fill, I thought that my friend who was ailing was staying at Tianning Temple. Instead of spending money in a noisy inn to spend this long, lonely winter night, it would be better to go to the ancient temple to talk to him. Moreover, I could also take the opportunity to inquire about his recent health, so I called the temple and asked them not to close the mountain gate too early.

I got back on the streetcar, and in the moonlight, as cool as water, I looked at the calm streets and alleys, and the changing stars, feeling a sense of loneliness on my journey. Thanks to the rickshaw puller's strength, he pulled me towards Dongzhi Street. I heard the sound of the watchman's gong on the city wall, slowly becoming lighter and farther away.

Round and round, I don't know how far we traveled. Because of fatigue, I just closed my eyes and let my thoughts wander. Although the cold wind easily awakens a light intoxication, I immersed myself in even deeper reverie, even vaguely forgetting to look at the buildings in the night.

It was when the rickshaw came out of the East Gate that, in the dim light of the oil lamps, I vaguely recognized three or five refugee beggars, squatting on straw and dozing off. So I completed a five-character poem: "Poor and drunk seek a haven, lonely footsteps happen to visit Zen. Frosty clothes draped over the noon moon, catkins press against my prime! On the road, I hear hungry birds, in the mansions, the sounds of music. It is our generation's concern to grieve for the times, but there is no way to ask the deaf heavens." I planned to recite it to my ailing friend after a while, to see how he would critique it.

Almost at the end of Dongzhi Street, the rickshaw puller suddenly asked, his voice sounding rushed,

"Sir, should I pull straight into Tianning Temple?"

This interrupted my contemplation of the poem.

Opening my eyes, I saw a gray battlement on the left, with a curved doorway in the center. The moonlight was pouring into the square inside the gate, where tall trees provided shade and appeared to be sleeping in clusters. As I pointed towards the mountain gate to the rickshaw puller, the rickshaw quickly rolled inside.

I don't know if it was because of the sound of the rickshaw bell, or the accidental night cry of a roosting bird, but it startled a sleeping yellow dog, which jumped up and barked furiously. In the quiet night, it was easy to disturb the gate-keeping monk.

At this time, a frozen cloud was flying across the sky, temporarily obscuring the moon. In the empty courtyard, there was only a deep darkness, and the leaves were singing in the wind. Along with the dog's barking, the scene was truly touching. Looking towards the mountain gate ahead, a small red light was faintly visible, seeming to be moving, moving very quickly, like a lighthouse in the night sea. But the light moved closer and closer, and bigger and bigger. Gradually, I could see the face of the person holding the lantern. Wasn't it a monk wearing a tall hat? I immediately jumped off the rickshaw, paid the fare, and hurried towards the red light by the tree, gratefully saying:

"Master, I'm so sorry to trouble you! You've been waiting a long time."

"It's alright! Are you coming from the city, sir?" The monk stood still and asked me in return. (To be continued)

Page 16

Ten Questions and Ten Answers 216

(1) Doctor Zhao asks: I have been practicing medicine for many years, but I have not found any perfect medical books to reference, which is a great regret. You have lived in Shanghai for a long time and must have seen and heard a lot. Can you tell me something? Answer: The Guangxie Bookstore at No. 140 Beijing Road, Shanghai (corner of Route Pottier) sells books of this type from the Chinese Medical Association (formerly the Bo Medical Association) and the Chinese Nurses Association. There should be everything you need. You may wish to write for a catalog to read. (2) Principal Li asks: Our school has many students and plans to implement the New Life Movement, focusing on hygiene. Where can we purchase hygiene books? Answer: The Guangxue Bookstore in Shanghai sells all hygiene books, charts, models, and lantern slides from the Chinese Hygiene Education Association, the Ministry of Interior's Department of Health, and major bookstores. The styles are complete and purchasing is extremely convenient.

(3) Ms. Huang Lizhu asks: There are more than a dozen infants and young children in my home, who often get sick, causing both mental and financial losses. Is there any wonderful way to remedy this? I hope you can advise me! Answer: Infants get sick mostly because parents do not know how to prevent them, and after they get sick, they do not know how to take good care of them. If you have books such as the Childcare Guide (one yuan), Haohou and Ershi's Infant and Pediatric Medicine, Volumes I and II (nine yuan), Hao Ci's Pediatric Q&A (two jiao), Infant Nursing Methods (four jiao), or Healthy Living (five yuan), they can be of great help. The above books are sold by Guangxue Bookstore. (4) Colonel Zhang Mingda asks: Mingda has served in the Army Hospital for three years and now plans to study surgery and anatomy. Are there any perfect Chinese texts? Answer: Guangxie Bookstore has a large number of medical books of this kind. You can write a letter to ask for a catalog.

(5) Mr. Wang Boqin asks: I have been studying at a medical school late in life, and I see that there are no standard translations of medical terms, which causes some difficulties when studying and translating. Is there a bookstore in Shanghai that sells standard medical dictionaries? Answer: The standard medical terminology dictionaries reviewed and approved by the Scientific Terminology Review Committee include Medical Terminology Compilation, eight yuan; English-Chinese Medical Vocabulary, four yuan; Chinese-English Medical Dictionary, two and a half yuan; Chinese Pharmacopoeia, six yuan. All are sold at Guangxie Bookstore, No. 140 Beijiu Road, Shanghai.

(6) Professor Di Zilin asks: I have long known that Guangxie Bookstore is the general agency for Chinese medical and health books. However, I like to read original foreign books. I don't know if there is a bookstore in Shanghai that sells them? Answer: The Oxford University Press and the Columbia University Press in New York publish a wealth of medical books. Guangxie Bookstore is the Chinese manager of these two companies. The bookstore also sells medical books from other major British and American bookstores.

(7) Miss Xue Huifen asks: After class, I often like to sing poems and play the piano to entertain myself. Now I plan to add more sheet music and songbooks to increase my enjoyment. I would appreciate it if you could introduce some good books! Answer: The sheet music used by famous girls' schools such as Shanghai Zhongxi Girls' School and St. Mary's are mostly purchased from Guangxie Bookstore. Therefore, the young lady can also purchase from the bookstore.

(8) Pastor Chen asks: The church members in my area are eager to read various Christian publications in order to understand the truth and preach the gospel. However, there are many publishing agencies, and it often takes a lot of time to purchase a book by mail, asking questions repeatedly, and the result is still nothing. Is there a simple and effective way to purchase by mail? Answer: There are about a hundred Christian publishing agencies, large and small. Shanghai Guangxie Bookstore has spared no effort to collect more than ten thousand kinds of new and old books published by them and compiled an index (Chinese-English combined, one yuan; Chinese version, two jiao). With this book, the book title can be established and purchased from Guangxie Bookstore, which is extremely convenient. (9) Mr. Ge Shangjie asks: I have some experience in English and find that reading the original English version is more pure and natural. However, it is quite inconvenient to order from abroad every time. Is there a bookstore in Shanghai that manages British publications? Answer: The publications of Oxford University Press are world-famous, and the publications of more than ten other companies such as Columbia University Press are all managed by Guangxie Bookstore. In addition to literature, it also sells specialized scientific books.

(10) Dr. Zhang Chengdao asks: Is the name of the central agency in our country that sells medical and health books Guangxue Bookstore or Guangxie Bookstore? Answer: It was originally named Guangxue Bookstore. Later, because the name was easily confused with Guangxuehui, the Guangxie Bookstore is still located at No. 140 Beijing Road, Shanghai (corner of the Museum Road). Also, because the bureau took over the Xiehe Bookstore, it was renamed.

Western Academy of Sciences Collects Specimens, Yu Jichuan Talks About the Discovery of New Plants in Xikang 217

Ruide Wood and Gongtong Discovered on High Mountains

Liangshan Yi Nationality Kidnaps Han People as Slaves

(Special dispatch from Peiping) Yu Jichuan, chairman of the Botany Department of the Western Academy of Sciences, arrived in Peiping from Sichuan today, carrying more than twenty boxes of plant specimens collected in Sichuan. He will borrow the Jing Sheng Biological Survey Institute to test and determine their functions and types. This afternoon, the reporter visited Yu. According to him, the Western Academy of Sciences was initiated by Lu Zuofu and others, and was established in Baxian, Sichuan in 1931. The main tasks are investigation, research, experimentation, and improvement of Western products. There are currently biological, physical and chemical, geological, and agricultural and forestry research institutes. The biological and geological research institutes focus on investigation. In addition to private fundraising, the China Culture and Education Foundation Committee also provides some subsidies. The responsibility I (Yu himself) undertake is the botany department, so I can only tell you about the situation of the botany department. The main task of the botany department is to investigate wood, medicinal materials, oil materials, and other main tasks. Sichuan has the most of these items, so it is divided into early areas, and it is planned to complete the three investigations. The general purpose since 1932 is to (1) solve the types of plants, (2) the economic value of plant species. Although the scheduled period has expired, there are still some that have not been completed, so supplementary work is still being done. Later, because Xikang is adjacent to Sichuan Province and there are few people who go there for health surveys, people have recently been sent to collect plant specimens. The province is divided into four regions, which are expected to be completed within two years. There may be new discoveries in the future to contribute to the academic community. As for the plants collected in Sichuan Province, more than ten new species have been discovered and announced. The most recently discovered new species include Ruide Wood, Gongtong, and Rhododendron (Azalea). The first two must be found on high mountains of two or three kilometers or more. What are their functions? Still under study. In mid-August and September last year, the botany department sent personnel to the mountains southwest of Sichuan to collect specimens. The area is located between Sichuan Leibo, Mabian, Ebian, Pingshan, Xichang, and Huili, which are occupied by the Yi nationality. They are very harmful to the exclusion of the Han people. Only small merchants go there at ordinary times, so the people of Sichuan are all regarded as secret dens. Before we went, we had the help of the highest local government and the gentry of the neighboring counties, and we bought off the responsible protection of the three branches of Moshimoqu Enxia (that is, the chiefs) with Sichuan salt and local cloth before we dared to go. We stayed there for two months and collected many specimens and discovered large forests, about a hundred miles long and about twenty miles wide, and drew maps of the deep mountains. However, we encountered many difficulties, and some lives were sacrificed along the way, so we could not complete the work. The local people occupied Zhaojue County in Sichuan Province, and often kidnap Han people as slaves and can buy and sell them at will. Therefore, the Han people who are now in the area account for 80 to 90 percent of the total population and are generally assimilated. If the Chinese people continue to be as indulgent as they used to be, the Yi nationality will harm Sichuan Province, and I am afraid it will be even worse than the Communist bandits, said (Jin).

The Second Day of the Working Discussion Meeting of the Social Education Guidance Institutions in Zhejiang Province 219

The provincial social education guidance institution working discussion meeting held by the Zhejiang Education Department continued yesterday (the 17th) in the auditorium of the Education Department. The attendees gathered at 8:00 a.m., presided over by Section Chief Jiao of the third section of the Education Department. The meeting began as usual. First, the chairman reported on the future direction of Zhejiang Province's promotion of social education, followed by Lin Mu, the principal of the People's Education Experimental School, who spoke on the past, present, and future of Zhejiang Province's training of people's education talents. In the afternoon, they discussed eleven proposals put forward by the Provincial People's Education Museum, including establishing the central cause of people's education in this province, conducting regional pilot studies on the work of the people's education center, the liaison method between the provincial social education institutions and the provincial school district social education guidance institutions, linking party and government construction and agricultural institutions to hold rural revitalization demonstration areas, the guiding principles of the provincial school district social education guidance institutions, the implementation of education and cultivation in equal measure, how education should effectively communicate with relevant institutions, how to actively conduct civic training when holding Baojia, and the county and city people's education museums and people's schools should consider relocating to rural areas.
