Ministry of Education Compiles Chinese Education Yearbook 220

To Publicize to the International Community to Clarify the Truth of Education in Our Country

The Ministry of Education approved a letter from the International English Yearbook Agency, requesting that a summary of Chinese education be compiled in 200,000 words and translated into Western languages ​​in order to publicize to the international community. Because international organizations often do not understand the situation of Chinese education when editing the education yearbooks of various countries in the world, there is no systematic record of the whole thing. Therefore, China compiles a national education yearbook similar to the entire systematic education summary and sends it to the agency. After receiving the letter, the Ministry of Education has compiled the characteristics and summary of higher, secondary, primary, and social education at all levels throughout the country. It is being translated by members of the Ministry who are proficient in English. The English version will be completed soon and a letter will be sent to the agency for international promotion.

Ministry of Education Explains the Deadline for Repeat Grades for Students Who Fail the Joint Entrance Examination 221

The Ministry of Education, in order to explain the deadline for students who fail the joint entrance examination to repeat grades, instructed the Jiangsu Education Department, stating briefly that the deadline for repeating grades for the secondary school graduation joint entrance examination should be handled in accordance with Article 64 of the Secondary School Regulations. (Article 64 stipulates that students who fail more than three subjects in the graduation joint entrance examination or only two subjects fail, but the subjects are any two of the four subjects of Chinese, English, arithmetic, and work in junior high school, and any two of the five subjects of Chinese, English, arithmetic, physics, and chemistry in senior high school shall be required to repeat the grade for one year. However, this repetition is limited to one time. If they still cannot graduate, a certificate of completion will be issued and they will be required to withdraw from school.)

Ten Professors to Hold First Cultural Construction Seminar Today 229

Invite Reporters from Various Newspapers and Professors from Various Universities to Participate

Hoping That This Meeting Will Produce Concrete Solutions

Cai Yuanpei Writes to He Bingsong in Support of the Principles of the Declaration

The ten professors who recently published the Declaration on Chinese-Based Cultural Construction are now scheduled to hold the first Cultural Construction Seminar at the Central Society at 5:00 pm today to discuss various issues of cultural construction. Those who have been invited to participate include chief writers of various newspapers, presidents of various universities, and more than 30 well-known scholars. The record will be published in the fifth issue of the Cultural Construction Monthly. After publication, opinions from various scholars will be solicited. It is hoped that more concrete opinions will be produced so that this movement will not become an impractical movement. Also, He Bingsong, who signed the declaration, had previously sent the declaration to Cai Yuanpei. Cai now has a reply, acknowledging that the principles in the declaration are unbreakable principles and hoping that he can go further and strive to materialize the two principles of not being conservative and not blindly following. The original letter is specially published as follows:

Mr. Bocheng's Da Jian, I have read the Declaration on Chinese-Based Cultural Construction that you sent me. In principle, in abstract theory, it can be said to be unbreakable. Confucius said, "When three men are walking together, there must be one who can serve as my teacher. I choose his virtues and follow them; his vices, I correct them." This is the attitude of not being conservative and not blindly following. The most important task now is to choose the good. What is good, what is universally recognized as good by mankind, without the distinction between Chinese and non-Chinese? What is considered good by the Chinese but not considered good by the non-Chinese? What is considered good by the non-Chinese but not considered good by the Chinese? List these objects separately, then compare and study them, which should be taken, which should be abandoned. Systematically compile the components that should be taken, and then a cultural construction plan can be made, and then the remaining characteristics of China can be pointed out. If there is no such plan and you discuss it out of thin air, it will inevitably be like Zhang Zhidong's slogan "Chinese Learning for the Fundamental Principles, Western Learning for Practical Application" and Liang Shuming's "Eastern and Western Cultures." Whether you agree or disagree, it is all empty talk. I respectfully present my humble opinion for your reference. Respectfully, Cai Yuanpei respectfully inscribed on January 18, 1935.

Yu Tang Cooperative Members' Congress 233

Amending the Cooperative Charter and Electing Supervisors

Distributing Profits and a Festive Dinner

The Shanghai Yu Tang Agricultural Production, Transportation, Marketing, Purchasing, Utilization, Credit, and Guarantee Cooperative was established in the 19th year [of the Republic, i.e., 1930] under the advocacy of Mr. Niu Yangsheng. The former Agricultural and Mining Department of Jiangsu Province appointed Mr. Feng Zanyuan and Mr. Min Zhongji to be stationed in Yu Tang to design and guide its development. Since then, its foundation has become increasingly solid and its scale has broadened daily. Not only is it a model for various counties in Shanghai and Songjiang, but it has also been evaluated by the Construction Department of Jiangsu Province as number one among the 61 counties in the province. Recently, the cooperative added large-scale oil pressing equipment in its utilization department and implemented production cooperation, hoping to integrate various aspects of its business to accelerate the cooperative function, in order to assist in the improvement of rural affairs. The cooperative, in accordance with its charter, recently convened a members' congress. One hundred and fifty-six members attended, gathering at the Yu Tang People's Education Hall at 12 noon. After lunch, the meeting commenced. First, the Chairman of the Board of Directors, Wang Chengyao, led the attendees in performing the rituals, followed by a report on the general situation of the cooperative's affairs over the past year. Subsequently, department heads such as Niu Zhiyi gave separate reports. Then, Niu Tisheng, representing Gu Jiaxuan, Niu Changyao, Chairman of the Yu Tang Cooperative Enterprise Guidance Committee, Feng Guohua, Director of the Provincial People's Education Hall Experimental Zone, and Feng Zanyuan, Director of the Livelihood Department, gave speeches. This was followed by a discussion of proposals: (1) to amend the cooperative charter to add articles for corporate members, (2) to approve 15 new members and recognize the Maqiao Cooperative and Qingdeng Cooperative as corporate members, (3) to elect Huang Meixian, Niu Changyao, Wang Aire and others as supervisors for this session. Then the distribution of profits took place, totaling more than 1,357 yuan. After deducting the public reserve fund, public welfare fund, reserve fund, and cooperative share interest according to the regulations, all the rest was distributed. After the meeting, a dinner was held. At 6 o'clock, the Yu Tang People's Education Hall, Yu Tang Elementary School, Qiangnu Horticultural School, and Yu Tang Drama Society performed entertainment, and the event ended with joy around 10 o'clock.

(6) The association will provide meals and accommodation for the participating students, who must bring their own luggage and stay in designated locations. Meal tickets will be issued by the association for dining at designated restaurants. (10) Participating members must undergo an oral examination by the head of the class at the end of the training period. The Withstand Voltage Problem of Filter Capacitors (Li Yuanqing) 244

Recently, I and a friend repaired several AC radios of different styles. Some were purchased ready-made, and some were assembled by ourselves. However, the problems we found were exactly the same: the filter capacitor (Filter Condenser) short-circuited due to overload. Isn't this a very strange thing?

Commercially available radios, in order to strive for small size and low price, have to minimize the volume and quantity of each component. Therefore, it is natural that their filter capacitors are not durable. But why do self-made radios also have the same problem? That's a bit puzzling!

I guess that many people still don't have a good understanding of the withstand voltage problem of filter capacitors!

We know that all capacitors have a certain withstand voltage (Voltage rating), and exceeding this specified voltage is enough to affect its lifespan. This is an undeniable fact.

The withstand voltage marked on a capacitor usually represents the DC voltage, not the AC voltage. If you don't believe it, try connecting a capacitor marked with a withstand voltage of 500 volts to a 500-volt AC circuit, and there will likely be a short circuit soon!

To explain the above special phenomenon, we must first talk about the AC voltage itself.

The so-called AC voltage is not as simple as DC voltage. Strictly speaking, it is meaningless to just say "AC voltage." You must specify what kind of AC voltage it is.

The AC voltage itself is a sinusoidal waveform (Sine wave Form). (See attached picture) Its value changes constantly at any moment, and it is not constant. For the convenience of use, people divide it into the following three values:

(1) Effective AC Voltage: As mentioned above, AC voltage changes at any moment. In this way, isn't it difficult for us to get a definite value? In order to solve this difficulty, scientists first specified that the value of AC voltage that can produce the same function as DC voltage is called effective AC voltage (Effective Value of A. C. Voltage). The so-called AC voltage or the value measured in the AC voltage meter usually belongs to this type. Its value is approximately 0.707 times the maximum AC voltage.

(2) Maximum AC Voltage: The so-called maximum AC voltage (Maximum Value of A. C. Voltage) is the value of the AC voltage at its peak, so it is also called peak voltage (Peak Voltage). Its value is approximately 1.41 times the effective value.

(3) Average AC Voltage: The average AC voltage mentioned here (Average Value of A. C. Voltage) does not refer to the average value of the AC voltage in one cycle (Cycle) (the average value of one cycle is exactly zero), but refers to half a cycle (such as C to D and F to G in the figure). Its value is approximately 0.9 times the effective value.

The value measured in the AC voltage meter is the effective value, not the maximum value, as mentioned above. In fact, the maximum value can still be encountered twice in each cycle. Therefore, when using capacitors or any other components in AC circuits, we must be able to withstand the maximum value. In other words, it must be able to withstand at least 1.41 times the effective value to be applicable. From this point of view, it can be seen that connecting a 500-volt capacitor in an AC circuit means that the voltage it actually receives has a maximum of 500 * 1.41 = 705 volts, exceeding its specified withstand voltage by almost half, so how can there be no danger?

For example, if the output tube of a certain radio is 45, when the screen voltage is 275 volts, the C voltage is about 56 volts. Assuming that the voltage drop in the low-frequency choke coil is 40 volts, then the effective voltage received by the filter capacitor has reached 371 volts, and its maximum value is 375 x 1.41 = 523.11 volts. Under this condition, if a 500-volt capacitor is recklessly connected, it is expected that it will not be durable.

Sometimes, if the external voltage is too high, or the waveform is distorted (Wave Dislortion) due to the transformer heating up, its maximum value often exceeds 1.41 times the effective value. Therefore, in AC circuits, various insulation materials are usually used, and for safety reasons, the standard is that they can withstand 1.5 times the effective value. Therefore, the above-mentioned capacitor should use one that can withstand 371 x 1.5 = 556.15 volts. You can choose one that is closest to this number and can withstand 700 volts (Note: The withstand voltage marked on the capacitor is usually an advertising claim. In fact, it must be discounted by at least 80% to 90%. Therefore, choosing a 700-volt capacitor is not too much.

In addition, the withstand voltage of a capacitor will also be affected by heat. Therefore, the position where the capacitor is placed in the radio should be as far away as possible from the power transformer and other heating parts such as vacuum tubes. This also needs to be explained in passing.

Converting Powerful AC Radios to Headphones (Ming Xiang) 245

Since the popularity of powerful AC radios, headphones seem to have become relics of the past. Those who prepared them earlier now abandon them like waste. In fact, in many cases, we often feel the need for headphones. For example, when listening to music late at night, using a speaker to play music will inevitably disturb people's dreams. It is better to switch to headphones for quietness. Comrades who like to play with shortwave, if they use a speaker to receive music from distant radio stations, often get nothing because the signal is too weak. If they can switch to headphones, it is not difficult to get unexpected gains. If there are elderly people or people with hearing impairments at home, others may not be able to distinguish the appropriate volume when it is adjusted to the appropriate level. It is best to split a headphone so that they can also enjoy the music.

This article describes two of the simplest methods that can make headphones suitable for any radio. The first method is to add a wire to the screen of the last stage output tube of the radio: A is connected to the shell (Figure 1), and is connected to one end of a single-track headphone jack through a blocking capacitor C.

The other end is connected to the radio shell, as shown in Figure 1A. The jack can be installed on the side of the radio wooden box. If the output stage uses two vacuum tubes connected in push-pull mode, the two ends of the jack must each be connected to the screens of the two vacuum tubes through a blocking capacitor, as shown in Figure 1B.

When using, just insert the headphone plug into the jack to listen. As for the adjustment procedures of the radio, they are still the same as usual. If you want to receive distant radio stations, you only need the headphones to make sound. You can add a switch to the speaker voice coil wiring to turn it off. If you add headphones specifically for people with hearing impairments, you can turn on the switch and the speaker will play sound at the same time.

The volume adjustment of the first method must be adjusted on the original volume controller of the radio. The volume in the headphones cannot be adjusted separately, which is very inconvenient. Therefore, there is a second method to remedy this, that is, the headphones are not directly inserted into the radio's jack, but are replaced by a volume controller, as shown in Figure 2. The ab ends can receive the jack on the radio, and the headphones are inserted into J2 to adjust R, so that the volume in the headphones is suitable for their personal needs.

Amplifying Frequency Range Difference KMK 246

Whether it is a radio or an amplifier, if you want it to have sufficient volume output, you must have considerable amplification equipment. Ordinary amplification is divided into high-frequency amplification (Radio Frequency Amplifier), intermediate frequency amplification (Intermediate Frequency)

Ampjilier) and low-frequency amplification (Audio Frequency Amplifier) and other three types of high-frequency amplification are to amplify the high-frequency radio waves emitted by the broadcasting station. After being amplified by the tube, the output is still high-frequency radio waves. The principle is nothing more than strengthening external radio signals to make the detection stage easier to receive.

Intermediate frequency amplifiers are mostly used in heterodyne or super-heterodyne radios. The so-called intermediate frequency is already the result of a considerable amount of detection. This detection is called the first-stage detection. Although the high-frequency radio waves have been detected, the signals received by the human ear cannot be heard. Therefore, intermediate frequency amplification is added here. It is also adjusted between the mutual inductance of the two coils, and then becomes an audio low frequency through the second-stage detection. Because there are many adjustment parts in this method, the selectivity is excellent.

Low-frequency amplification is to amplify the detected audio low-frequency radio waves. The amplification effect of this method is greater than the previous two methods, but the selectivity is of course inferior to the previous method because the adjustment part cannot be added. If multi-stage low-frequency amplification is added, the tone will inevitably be distorted. Therefore, in imported radios, low-frequency amplification is at most only one stage.

The Latest Tone Control Method (Li Yuanqing) 247

The usual method of controlling the tone is probably to connect a fixed capacitor and a variable resistor in parallel in the low-frequency amplification circuit (primary or secondary). When used, reducing the resistance can cut off the higher-frequency tones (Cut). As a result, the sound emitted from the speaker becomes very dull. (Please refer to my previous work "Tone Control Method" in issue 16 of this publication)

"Tone Control," as the name implies, should be able to control the high and low tones at will. However, the above-mentioned tone controller can only delete the high frequencies and fully release the low frequencies, but cannot reduce the low frequencies and emit high frequencies as much as possible. This is its shortcoming!

Western music has a high-pitched tone and many instruments. Whenever twenty or thirty people play together, the sound is loud and there is a lot of noise. Therefore, the high-frequency sound waves must be deleted before it can be pleasing to the ear. Chinese music is not like this. For example, a Dan role sings opera with a Jinghu. It is already monotonous. If you add the above-mentioned tone controller, then the listener will think that the person is playing a broken Huqin and singing with a nasal voice. This is the difference between the organization of Chinese and Western music and the hearing of Chinese and Western people. It cannot be forcibly combined.

Recently, I saw a new type of tone controller in the British Amateur Wireless magazine, which can remedy the above-mentioned shortcomings. I have translated it succinctly for the reference of enthusiasts.

As shown in the figure, L is a 3 to 4 bv choke coil, C is a 0.1 mf fixed capacitor, and R is a 10,000-ohm potentiometer (all connected in parallel in the primary coil of the low-frequency transformer, as shown in the dotted line in the attached figure). When the potentiometer R stops at the center point, this device has little effect. At this time, the tone released from the speaker is moderately high and low. When R is turned to the right, the higher-frequency tones all slip away from C, and the sound emitted is very dull. When R is turned to the left, the lower-frequency tones all escape from L, and the sound emitted can be very lively.

Another Method to Increase Selectivity KMK 248

In Shanghai, where there are many radio stations, the issue of selectivity is indeed difficult to solve. Except for multi-stage high-frequency adjustment and super-heterodyne radios with better selectivity, the selectivity of ordinary circuit radios is particularly bad, and even four or five are mixed together. In addition to shortening the antenna, reducing the primary coil, and adjusting the antenna circuit, there seems to be no other way to solve the above-mentioned problem. Now the author will introduce a very good method to increase selectivity, which I think will be welcomed by readers! The circuit is shown in the figure. L is the primary circuit coil, L is the regenerative regeneration coil, L2 is the external adjustment coil, and L3 is the grid circuit coil (that is, the secondary circuit coil). The selectivity is excellent according to the design of the figure. The coil can be wound on the spider web board with No. 26 enameled wire. L must be wound more than the ordinary one, and L1 must be determined according to the characteristics of the vacuum tube. L2 and L3 are each wound with 65 turns. Arrange them in the order of the figure, and fix the distance between them after appropriate testing. C and C are both 0.00035 MF variable capacitors.

Small Experience: Method to Eliminate Vibration Noise of Power Supply Square Iron Plate (Zhou Wenhuan) 249

The power supply square plate occupies an important position in AC radios (although there are some that do not use it now, but they are still a minority). Its working performance (that is, no heat generation, no vibration noise, etc.) has a great relationship with the sound performance of the machine. The author recently repaired a machine for a friend, and his problem is what I am going to tell you. The machine was assembled by himself with purchased parts. The circuit is a three-tube powerful AC machine. The power supply square plate is also self-made. The volume and selectivity are not bad, but the most hateful thing is that the AC sound is very loud. But after checking its interior, the places where AC sound can be eliminated have been changed, and there is no way to solve it. After I got it for repair, I immediately checked it and found that the iron plates on the west side of the square plate core were slightly vibrating. Pressing it with my hand would reduce the AC sound. At that time, I was sure that it must be the cause of the problem. How to cure it? The method is very simple: just use white wax liquid (that is, wax candles, etc.) and melt it into the gaps of the iron plates. Once it cools down, connect to the power supply, and the hateful AC sound disappears. If any of the readers have the same problem, you may wish to try it. If three-tenths of beeswax can be added to the above-mentioned white wax liquid, it will not become ineffective immediately if the square plate heats up.

Wheat Initially Steady, Then Falls 260

Yesterday's wheat futures market showed a trend of initial stability followed by declines in all months after opening in the morning. The prices of foreign wheat were up about 0.1 to 0.2 yuan in both Chicago and Canada. When the opening price was announced, the market was stable because the foreign wheat price was favorable. Shandong Guide Mingguang wheat opened at 3.84 yuan, and Fuxin Company purchased it.

The drought and cold in the southwest of Chicago wheat are now being discussed by the general public. The market is showing a trend where both gains and losses are possible. Neither the long nor the short sides intend to increase their positions.

Rice Market Stable in the South, Weak in the North 261

(Shanghai South) Yesterday's arrivals totaled over 40 boats, with a total of 7-8,000 shih of goods. Sales increased slightly as the market had dropped sharply the day before and the prices of various goods seemed to have bottomed out. Sales were seen on this street and Qingdao merchants continued to purchase 6-700 bags. Therefore, the overall trend was stable and slightly tight. Late rice and various thick japonica prices were stable except for the high-grade varieties, some of which had risen slightly. Dujian and Bianyin Yuan and other varieties also stabilized.

(Shanghai North) Yesterday's arrivals from various places downriver totaled over 30 boats. Sales of white japonica short grain were slightly easier. Sales of thin rice Bian Yuan were mediocre and sales of various pointed grains were sluggish. Market prices for high-grade white japonica fell by 0.1 yuan and medium and lower grades fell by 0.01-

The Supply of Soybean Oil in the Oil Market Cannot Meet Demand 262

丨Soybean Cakes Also Continue to Rise丨

Recently, the market conditions for peanut oil and soybean oil have been such that, due to the lack of supply sources and the gradual depletion of inventories, prices have generally been increasing per unit. However, yesterday's market was influenced by continuous price increases reported from Dalian, leading to tight purchasing in the market. Only a few sellers were able to supply demand, causing a sharp rise in prices. Peanut oil increased by twenty cents, and soybean oil increased by forty cents. The overall outlook remains positive. Since inquiries for soybean cakes from Shantou merchants began, the market for soybean cakes has been quite strong. Yesterday, the spot price for 'Four Brands' soybean cake opened at $1.44.

The Trading of Hardware and Lead Still Struggles to Improve 263

The trading of lead has always been most active among red lead factories, paint companies, tin foil factories, and type-setting rooms. Since tea merchants switched to using zinc sheets, the number of lead boxes they require has also decreased, resulting in a less vibrant market than before. In recent months, the market has been sluggish due to oversupply. Despite repeated efforts by businesses to find solutions and promote sales, the adverse environment has hindered any real improvement in trading. Here is a breakdown of market conditions from various merchants:

(Foreign Lead) Arrivals have been frequent recently, resulting in a significant accumulation in the warehouses. However, there has been no activity from local merchants, and only a minimal amount of business from local factories. The resulting market quietness is difficult to describe. Although businesses have been actively promoting sales, the end of the year brings tight credit conditions, preventing large-scale transactions. The market price is estimated at $15.20 per dan (unit), with little change compared to the previous period. A small amount of trading is reported at prices ranging from $15.40 to $15.50.

(Domestic Lead) Although the quantity of arrivals is not high, the limited sales outlets have also made the market quite sluggish. The market price is estimated at $14.70 to $14.80 per dan. Retail sales to smaller shops are priced around $15.00. Daily transactions are only sporadic with few wholesale deals. It is rumored that there is still a large quantity of spot goods in Hankou that can be shipped, causing a sense of weakness in the local market. It is anticipated that the market price may soften in the future.

Miscellaneous Talks

Protecting Other Species Should Start with Protecting One's Own Kind by Xing An 271

Human behavior is always contradictory. Like now, on the one hand, some people are desperately manufacturing airplanes, cannons, and poisonous gases, shouting hoarsely, "Kill! Kill! Kill!" On the other hand, some people are enthusiastically promoting animal protection, expressing sympathy to animals with benevolence.

However, contradictory as it may be, in today's world, even though some people are holding a large bomb in their hands, aiming it at the head of the god of peace and throwing it away, people with a heart may as well develop their own compassionate nature. Just because others are cruel, do we have to be cruel with them? Just because Wang Er next door does bad things, Zhang Wu here should do some good things to influence him. Otherwise, this human world will really turn into hell!

However, for humans, who claim to be the spirits of all things, to now pity and protect those animals that we have long regarded as straw dogs may not be a kind of awakening for humanity: however, this kind of awakening, initiated in the current world of the survival of the fittest, is indeed premature. Because now, humans cannot love each other, let alone extend love to other species? Therefore, I believe that protecting animals today is only a kind of thought of us humans, and it is still far from being realized. If we want to realize this ideal, the prerequisite should be to start with loving one's own kind.

This is an undeniable fact that the phenomenon of humans killing each other is more severe than in any animal kingdom. The hatred between countries and between races is obvious and easily seen: even people of the same country and the same race often stand in opposition and are incompatible. To put it mildly, it is not uncommon for families A and B to cause great disasters because of minor reasons.

Even with close relationships such as father and son, brothers, and husbands and wives, the affection between flesh and blood should be so deep; however, once they turn against each other, they often do not hesitate to resort to the last resort to deal with each other. This is a bad nature of mankind.

Because humans have this kind of bad nature, they cannot love each other. For a human being who does not even know how to love his own kind, it is impossible for them to bestow grace on other animals and protect them. Therefore, we believe that if humans really have a compassionate heart and are willing to care for animals, the first step should be to start by transforming human nature:

The Sorrow of a University Professor by Jiong Nv Shi 272

As soon as I stepped into the home of Professor Mou of the university, I saw him and his wife sitting side by side at a rectangular desk, busily compiling the lecture notes for Professor Mou's class. A kind of sorrowful expression was displayed on the face of the university professor. Frowning, with a sad face, as if something was on his mind. As soon as Professor Mou saw me, he put the pen in his hand on the desk and greeted me with a face full of smiles, and his wife also busily took out sweets for me to eat. "Where did you just come from? Did anything special happen at the school?" Professor Mou started asking me like this. "Because the professor didn't ask for leave and didn't attend class, I suspected that he was sick! Therefore, I came to visit." I replied aimlessly, which made everyone laugh. Professor Mou and I talked about school matters and personal living conditions. He told me in a very old-fashioned tone:

"A university professor is a signboard that sounds nice in name but is actually poor. I spend an immeasurable amount of energy, only to exchange it for meager living expenses. Think about it: during the day, I have to attend classes, and at night, I have to compile lecture notes and grade student papers: every night, I always have to stay up until midnight to sleep, I am simply sitting until my buttocks hurt. In order to make my position secure, I also have to deal with the school authorities and connect with students;

That kind of mental pain is simply indescribable!

What's more, the current life has no security, and I am constantly in a state of panic! Because the school's salary is not paid, I don't even have car fare these past two days, so,

Today, your homework has to be missed!" Professor Mou spoke to this point in one breath, his face seemed to be covered by a cloud of sorrow, appearing particularly dim! His wife also sighed uncontrollably.

Suddenly, a gust of wind blew in from the outside, blowing open the two doors. At this time, the sunlight had already hidden and was no longer on the stone steps just now. It was already approaching dusk. So I said goodbye to Mr. Mou and his wife.

Walking slowly on the way home, I still felt infinitely melancholy. So that's why Mr. Mou was absent from class today! Ah! The sorrow of a university professor!

Stimulation by Qun Ying 273

The bright moon is in the sky, the human shadow is on the ground, quietly returning alone from the road, passing through the small courtyard, seemingly reluctant to leave such a moonlit night, petrified and leaning against the corner of the wall, staring blankly at the clear sky without a cloud, all the sorrows in my heart seem to be washed away at once, slowly watching my own shadow rise and unfold from my heels, as if feeling a burst of chill, I then wearily went upstairs.

In the darkness, I felt my way to the door of the room from the corner, and unexpectedly, the door was wide open. I suddenly twisted the switch of the electric light. My old friend Wei was sleeping on the bed. On the small table beside the bed was a cup of tea, and a wisp of green smoke was still rising from the half-smoked cigarette butts in the ashtray. The alarm clock was pointing exactly at two o'clock. I suddenly remembered that I had invited him over tonight, wanting to steal a day of leisure next Sunday to make a short trip. Recently, I have really felt very tired of life, and every day I am mentally dazed like an insomniac, but there is absolutely no sign of illness. Of course, I know my own heart disease, but knowing is just knowing, and I have no ability to stir up my spirits. A week ago, I had passively immersed myself in dancing every night. At first, I seemed to enjoy those passionate music very much. Every time a piece of music played, I held a snake-like woman and dissipated my annoyance in the atmosphere inside. However, later it didn't have that kind of effect. I sat for two whole nights without dancing a single piece of music, which naturally caused many surprised and despicable glances to be cast at me, so I felt even more disgusted. I thought about asking Wei to leave this stinking metropolis, even if it was only for twenty-four hours on a Saturday.

But I slept a little late last night, opened the front window of the room, and felt that I had seen a moonlit night like this that I had not seen since I set foot in Shanghai, so I put on my autumn coat alone and wandered aimlessly in the moonlit night, walking through many secluded paths, the moonlight being filtered by the leaves of the maple trees beside the road into circles, and I just counted them as I moved forward. I also returned after midnight, and when I got to bed, I got a sweet dream. I also knew clearly that I was pursuing new stimulation, and it would be best to send my life to the kaleidoscope, so that I could live happily every day. Tonight, seeing the moonlight leaking in from the window frame, I went out alone again, but forgot to ask Wei to seek his agreement to the trip.

I slowly walked to the bedside. Wei woke up with a start, turned over, and grasped my hand. I knew he was going to question me about breaking our appointment, but my cold hand changed his question:

"Where did you come back from?"

"Looking at the moon."

Wei understood me best, and this answer was enough to satisfy him, so he didn't ask any more about these things, and directly talked about the reason why I had invited him.

"I want to go on a trip somewhere on Saturday."

"Good!"

Wei often encouraged me like this, and the greatness of friendship lies in this. He talked endlessly about the benefits of many scenic spots near Shanghai, although I clearly knew that he didn't know this in such detail.

"Okay, let's go to Wuxi."

"Okay! We'll take the night train on Saturday, and there will be a full day. And..." He said with a smile, "You've been too depressed lately, you should look for new stimulation. This week we'll travel, and next week I'll have new tricks..."

"Dancing in the ballroom!" I interrupted.

"Hmph: those women are too annoying. In short, I have a good place to go, I guarantee you'll be satisfied. You have to know that this is the boredom of young people!"

I said the last sentence softly in his ear,

I couldn't help but laugh.

Burning Toxic Substances Meng Ru 274

The other day, the Shanghai-Songhu Garrison Headquarters publicly burned all the toxic substances confiscated in previous drug cases. This was undoubtedly a resolute and heartening action. There are many reasons for China's decline, but the weakness of the people's physical health is the biggest fatal wound. If this fatal wound cannot be removed in the future, China may never be able to rise again. The root cause of the people's physical weakness is toxic substances. The government authorities, seeing this, have recently been strictly enforcing the prohibition of toxic substances without any leniency. We only need to look at the successive crackdowns on drug manufacturing facilities in Shanghai over the past few months to know a glimpse of the determination of the authorities. Soon, toxic substances will disappear, the people's health will gradually improve, and the entire country will embark on the road to strength.

However, things are not as optimistic as they seem. Our people have suffered from the scourge of toxic substances for a long time, and it cannot be eradicated overnight. Those who smoke have already become addicted, and it is difficult to quit without a strong will. Manufacturers often risk their lives and families to seek huge profits. The fact is right in front of us. Just a day or two after the burning of toxic substances in this city, didn't the authorities crack down on several more drug cases? This is a good illustration of how difficult it is to eradicate toxic substances.

There is another point that is a major obstacle to the future of drug prohibition. That is, a small number of foreigners often use their nationality as a talisman and their concessions as a safe haven to secretly organize drug manufacturing facilities, producing large quantities of toxic substances to harm our people. Their background is strong, their organization is tight,

their scale is large, and their manufacturing and trafficking are very skillful, making it difficult to crack down on them. Even if we occasionally discover them, they are not subject to our country's laws, so we cannot deter others from following suit.

However, are we discouraged about the prohibition of toxic substances? That's not the case. Although we face many difficulties in prohibiting toxic substances, we still have to find ways to overcome all the difficulties to achieve our goal. This requires the efforts of the authorities!

Home Bing Duo 275

Wanderers have no home.

I don't like to mention home in front of others, and I don't want to think of home alone. This is not because I want to forget my "drinking water, thinking of the source" home, because in fact, people living a wandering life, even if they miss and love it, is futile.

So, I can only say this.

The wandering life is the most annoying, the experience of sorrow and suffering in the human world especially makes every traveler's heart feel the misfortune of wandering and recall the gentle and comfortable home. Under the spring light of flowers competing for beauty, "the hometown is infinitely good" - who wouldn't think of the loveliness of home? In the lush green summer days, who can erase the pure interest of "fishing in the shade of trees" and "playing the flute in the wind"? When autumn comes, it is a refreshing weather again,

the light white clouds and the sad sound of rustling leaves, even more powerfully stir the wanderer's homesickness! Home in the depths of the white clouds!

However, precisely because I miss my home too much, and the life at home is too comfortable, I am afraid of thinking of home. My elderly father, dear brothers, and the love of blood are deeply etched in my heart. On the other hand, the decline of small-bourgeois families and the difficult financial situation at home make me worried and depressed. Because I am too concerned about family affairs and cannot escape the shackles of real life to return home, I simply don't want to think of home,

I don't want to talk about home! Even if I miss and love it, it is futile.

Since I cannot find a way to solve the difficult life at home, nor can I leave the wandering life and return home to live a loving and gentle life of family happiness. Forever living that sad wandering life, four years have passed, years like water. Since I left home that year.

Wanderers have no home.

I can only say this.

The Youthful Dream Cun Yin 276

The youthful dream has been blown away by the wind carrying fallen maple leaves. Gone, bit by bit! I don't know where to find it?

The youthful dream -- beautiful! Sentimental.

But I don't know where to find it!

Is it the awakening from a dream? Or has the dream vanished? Elusive! Go stand under the plane tree! Watch quietly! Watch the leaves of the plane tree fall!

Wherever the leaves fall, you should know where your dream has escaped!

So I gazed up angrily.

The leaves were blown down by the wind! One piece, two pieces, three pieces...

One piece floated into the gurgling stream.

One piece tumbled on the ground without stopping.

One piece was blown down and fell asleep in a stone crevice.

So many! So many leaves, each with a different destination. My dream? My dream? Oh, the youthful dream!

(I can't remember the year, the month, the day... when my dream began.

(I can't remember which mirror of copper and iron awakened my dream.

(I can't remember which gust of wind blew my dream away.

(Even more, I can't remember where my dream escaped?)

Suddenly, a series of familiar melodies, tenderly crept into my ears!

This is "My Dearest"!

How clear, my memories.

She had beautiful long hair -- like a rose fairy in a fairy tale.

She said:

I love a stray cat!

Because she's like a stray cat. Her walk is bouncy, her speech is quick, and she has a crisp laugh!

...Oh, and letter after letter -- beautiful handwriting!

The sound of the flute coming from afar, in this lonely night, is quite likely to arouse people's sorrow! The long sorrow is starting today! I remember it well.

In the sound of the flute, she bitterly complained about her own sadness and sorrow!

In the sound of the flute, tears flowed.

In the sound of the flute, we all took advantage of the moonlight's brightness,

paddled our oars, and separated. A vast expanse of white sea: watching her boat sail away. Similarly, she would also watch my boat become gradually smaller!

No one can hear anyone else's heavy sigh!

In this late night.

The youthful dream -- has awakened -- gone, bit by bit! I bid farewell to this dream and finally drifted to the "Land of Loneliness"!

This is a desolate cemetery! I'll stay here, burying my lively youthful life in vain! But I still carry a gloomy heart and dream of a "dream of light"!

The youthful dream. Beautiful! Sentimental.

Standard Great Man in Chinese History Yu Gong 277

In the past, a certain publication asked people to elect female great figures. Now, a certain cigarette company is asking people to elect standard great figures in history. The former included living people in the list of candidates. The latter is only open to the dead. The former was proposed by women, and women voted themselves. The latter is a merchant seeking profit in promoting his cigarettes. Since the motives are different, the nature is naturally different. The former election of female great figures had considerable value in encouraging female compatriots to improve. This time, the purpose is to enable students to receive scholarships, and the meaning of the election has already been lost.

Since the election itself has no meaning, it is close to a matter of "borrowing a topic to elaborate." This will not be discussed. It is just that the list of candidates cannot help but make people feel that it is a strange and interesting game.

I really admire the high opinion of the gentleman who decided on the list of candidates for this standard great man in history. Look how clearly he observed the general weaknesses of the Chinese people? Liu Bowen, who wrote "Tui Bei Tu" and "Shao Bing Ge," is worthless in the modern perspective of breaking superstitions, but he is the most worshipped figure among the Chinese people in this turbulent era, so he is a standard great man. Shen Baoxu, who sought foreign aid and cried at the Qin court, has nothing great about him. However, since the September 18th Incident, the Chinese people have been hoping that the gold-dollar imperialists would "draw their swords to help when they see injustice on the road"

and begged for assistance from the League of Nations Council, which was too busy to save itself. Shen Baoxu is a typical figure in history,

so he is also a standard great man.

However, in the list of candidates, there are also inexplicable arrangements, such as Zhou Yu, who was clearly the Grand Commandant of Eastern Wu, but is listed among the "civil officials." Zhuge Liang and Zeng Guofan are actually included in the "sages" category. Zhou Yu was probably harmed by his ability to listen to music and appreciate singing, so he is not worthy of being a military general. This may still make sense. How did Zhuge Liang and Zeng Guofan become standard great men of "sages"? Also, Zhang Zuolin and Jian Zhaonan have become "modern heroes." It is not known on what basis this is. Jian Zhaonan is the Chinese cigarette king. This is related to the cigarette company itself, so there is something to say. Zhang Zuolin became a "modern hero." Is this because he made meritorious contributions to the Republic of China as a warlord? This is probably the only reason. If the Beiyang warlord XXX had already "passed away," I think he would definitely be a great man among "modern heroes."

Suggestions for Promoting Domestic Fir Wood (Part Two) Shen Wen 283

(3) Points to note for the construction engineering industry

(A) Fir wood should be used first in construction engineering. According to the usual practice of design and drawing in construction,

foreign pine has uniform dimensions and standard strength. Ordinary wood, except for piles that must use round fir wood, is mostly foreign pine, because it is easy to calculate. However, foreign pine is a foreign product after all. Using one more piece means that one more piece of foreign pine money flows abroad. As long as the domestic fir wood of our country can withstand the same load-bearing force, it can be replaced and used. It is best to use fir wood even for larger dimensions. If special circumstances require the use of foreign pine, then foreign pine is still used. It is better than using all imported products.

(B) Test the strength of fir wood in the field. In European and Western countries, there are precise test standards for the strength of materials for design reference. My country's industry is still in its infancy. Although there are material testing facilities, domestic fir wood has not been tested in the field. There are still a lack of appropriate standards for elastic strength, fracture strength, elastic modulus, etc. At this time when domestic fir wood is being promoted, it should be tested urgently for design and material distribution reference.

(C) Organize a design research association for changing to round fir wood. Now that the strength of fir wood has been tested in the field, it is especially necessary to change the usual method of using square columns for drawing and design to using cylindrical methods, and to clearly define standards to facilitate implementation.

However, such standards cannot be reformed rashly without gathering wisdom and common research. Therefore, it is necessary to first organize a design research association for changing foreign pine to fir wood to discuss it.

(4) Points to be improved by fir wood merchants in the future

(A) Change the way of calculating by length to measuring diameter for pricing. As mentioned in the second article, fir wood valuation has too many complex shortcomings in calculation, which easily makes users abandon it. If measuring diameter pricing can be used to provide designers with a simple valuation, they will naturally be happy to use it.

(B) Purchase sawing machines to saw and sell various decoration application wood. Using foreign pine to saw and cut decorations often has the disadvantage of warping and cracking, which many users know. Using fir wood to make decorations can avoid this problem, but it is painful to waste labor and materials, which is not economical. If fir wood merchants can purchase machines to saw and sell ready-made wood for various parties to choose from, on the one hand, wholesale sawing and cutting can save labor costs, and on the other hand, the size of material loss and the sawing of different patterns do not require material loss, which is beneficial to both oneself and others.

(5) The authorities in the wood-producing area should be responsible for suppressing bandits to facilitate the source of goods.

I have heard from woodworkers that the construction of Guangxi's wood production areas is all in areas with rugged mountain roads and bandits出没. The transportation is tortuous. It is difficult for inexperienced mountaineers to go deep into the area. Often, the purchased rafts are robbed by bandits on the way. Extortion of huge sums of money, for this reason, mountain customers often hoard their goods and are unwilling to sell them cheaply. This is also an obstacle to the promotion of domestic wood. It is hoped that the authorities in the wood-producing area will find ways to annihilate the bandits and be responsible for escorting them. On the one hand, it is also hoped that miscellaneous taxes will be eliminated, so that the source of goods will be unblocked and the cost will be reduced, which can be sold all over the country.

The above five points are the points that all sectors of the promotion of domestic fir wood should pay attention to. In addition, the annual leakage of foreign pine is huge. It is expected that patriotic people with a little blood can be moved by reading it and know what to choose. I am ignorant and uneducated.

I feel it in my heart and write it down for a while, so I don't have time to take care of rhetoric. I hope that compatriots at home and abroad will earnestly promote domestic fir wood, and I ask the government to implement promotion and issue orders to the national engineering industry to use domestic products first when applying wood.

This is what I sincerely pray for. It is expected that the demand for fir wood will be huge, and lumber companies will stand tall, like bamboo shoots bursting out, although it cannot recover the past rights and interests, the large reduction in annual import surplus can be expected and awaited.

Architectural Weekly Huai Xiang 284

The Shandong Provincial Government, in the past, because the Confucius Temple in Qufu was severely damaged by artillery fire, and to worship the wise men and preserve the scenic spots, specially united with all sectors to organize a committee to repair the Confucius Temple in Qufu. The central government had resolved to allocate 100,000 national currency, and the donations from all parties were also quite considerable, but the cost was still huge. According to the report of Yang Jizuo of the Construction Department, after detailed investigation, there are three places on the roof of a tree (1) A clump of trees grows between the tiles of the front eaves of the Hall of Great Achievement (2) Four or five trees grow on the roof ridge behind the Dachen Gate (3) An elm tree grows between the tiles of the back eaves of the Kuiwen Pavilion, 3.5 meters high.

The Bank of China is preparing to build a new building, and is renovating the old house at the corner of Sichuan Road and Hankou Road, so that it can be temporarily moved into when building the new building. A large number of workers are rushing to install wires and water heaters. It is expected that all the work will be completed by the end of next month. The entire interior and exterior project is quite vast.

To prepare for the establishment of the National Central Museum, the entire construction cost of 1.5 million yuan was allocated by the Sino-British Boxer Indemnity Board of Directors, and the Ministry of Education and the Academia Sinica

jointly formed a preparatory committee, which appointed Li Ji as the director of the preparation. In order to facilitate construction planning and responsibility, the committee also established a construction committee, which appointed Weng Wenhao as the chairman, and Lei Zhen, Ding Wenjiang, and Zhang Daofan as members. The construction committee has decided to locate the site of the museum along Zhongshan Road.

The North China Games to be held tomorrow will be held on the recently completed North China Sports Field.

The entire building of the venue was designed by the Jintai Engineer.

A Building Soon to be Constructed on Park Road 285

At the corner of Park Road and Boone Road in this city, on the current site of Fuhuali, a tall, modern apartment building will soon be constructed after the demolition. The land was purchased by the British firm Keys & Doweswell. The architectural design is entirely by the firm. The front building will be seven stories high, and the rear building will be twice as tall, at fourteen stories. All plans have been approved by the Public Works Department and a construction tender will be issued soon.

The ground floor of the new building will be shops, and the upper floors will be spacious, modern apartments. The interior decoration and equipment will be as innovative as possible. The whole building will be magnificent. A glimpse can be seen in the drawings. The location is ideal, with convenient transportation, quiet amidst the bustling city. In the future, it will stand facing the International Hotel from afar. It will soon be filled with residents.

Therefore, architect Kwan Chung-sing returned to North China a few days ago. After the closing of the conference, he went south to preside over the construction of the Great China Company building in this city.

The Shanghai Fish Market, designed by architects Xu Jingzhi, Li Huibo, and Yang Runjun, is now ready for tender due to the availability of funds. The site has been determined as Zhoujiashui Island, Dinghai Bridge, Yangshupu, covering an area of more than 40 mu. The land is located along the Huangpu River, with deep water, allowing many fishing boats to dock. This tender is for the entire market construction, including (1) the fish market, (2) warehouses, (3) cold storage, etc. Those interested in undertaking this project should bring their business license and engineering management documents to the preparatory committee of the market at No. 33, Section 4, Sichuan Road in this city from October 6th to October 15th for verification. After approval, a deposit of 5,000 yuan and a drawing fee of 200 yuan should be paid to receive the drawings, specifications, tender regulations, etc. Bids must be submitted by the 23rd of this month for submission and selection.

Wuhan University has decided to build a law school. The Hubei Provincial Government will subsidize 120,000 yuan, and the Hunan Provincial Government has also agreed to allocate 5,000 yuan per month starting this month.

The Health Bureau is promoting model kitchens to encourage citizens to emulate them. A model kitchen will be built in the bureau first. The design has been completed and workers have been hired for construction. It will be completed soon. The internal equipment will be as simple and scientific as possible. The gate of Jiaotong University in Xujiahui in this city will be rebuilt. The design is by the Jietai Engineering Company. Contractors interested in undertaking the project can obtain tender regulations from the company at No. 113, 8th Floor, Jiujiang Road immediately.

The new building of the Pudong Native Place Association in this city, designed by architect Xi Fuquan, held a foundation laying ceremony at 2 pm on the 6th. About 800 people from Pudong and guests attended. After the opening speech by Du Yuesheng, the standing director of the association, the foundation laying ceremony was held.

Factory Building and Fire Prevention (2) Qin 286

(B) Automatic Fire Safety Equipment;

(1) Automatic fire extinguishing devices;

(2) Fire alarm reporting devices;

(3) Chemical fire extinguishers;

(4) Fire buckets and sand buckets;

(5) Ladders, iron hooks, etc.;

(6) Other rescue tools.

(C) Management Equipment;

(1) Organize a fire brigade. The number of members should be determined by the size of the factory. A fire chief should be appointed to lead them. If the fire brigade covers a large area, several squad leaders can be established, led by the chief;

(3) Training of firefighters;

(3) Training of general workers;

(4) Close liaison with the police authorities;

(5) Workers are not allowed to smoke while working. When resting, smoking must be done in the smoking room or in an open area;

(6) The chief should always inspect the workers' negligence and carefulness. Those firefighters who make efforts should be rewarded, otherwise, they should be punished;

(7) A separate annual fire protection expense should be set up in the accounting books.

The above is only a general description. Planners can choose and adopt it according to the different environments. I hope that industrialists can pay attention to this, so that unfortunate events can be gradually reduced every year. The investment of capitalists and the lives and property of workers should also be further guaranteed. This is the original intention of my writing this article. (End)
